CREATE TABLE "DOCLIGHT"."AB_GENERATED" 
   (	"TABLE_NAME" VARCHAR2(100), 
	"COLUMN_NAME" VARCHAR2(100), 
	"CONSTR" VARCHAR2(4000)
   ) SEGMENT CREATION IMMEDIATE 
  PCTFREE 10 PCTUSED 40 INITRANS 1 MAXTRANS 255 
 NOCOMPRESS LOGGING
  STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1
  BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT)
  TABLESPACE "USERS" ;
;

CREATE TABLE "DOCLIGHT"."D07_ERROR_LOOKUP" 
   (	"ID" NUMBER GENERATED BY DEFAULT ON NULL AS IDENTITY MINVALUE 1 MAXVALUE 9999999999999999999999999999 INCREMENT BY 1 START WITH 1 CACHE 20 NOORDER  NOCYCLE  NOKEEP  NOSCALE  NOT NULL ENABLE, 
	"CONSTRAINT_NAME" VARCHAR2(30 CHAR) NOT NULL ENABLE, 
	"MESSAGE" VARCHAR2(4000 CHAR) NOT NULL ENABLE, 
	"CREATED" DATE NOT NULL ENABLE, 
	"CREATED_BY" VARCHAR2(255 CHAR) NOT NULL ENABLE, 
	"UPDATED" DATE NOT NULL ENABLE, 
	"UPDATED_BY" VARCHAR2(255 CHAR) NOT NULL ENABLE, 
	 CONSTRAINT "D07_ERROR_LOOKUP_ID_PK" PRIMARY KEY ("ID")
  USING INDEX PCTFREE 10 INITRANS 2 MAXTRANS 255 COMPUTE STATISTICS 
  STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1
  BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT)
  TABLESPACE "USERS"  ENABLE
   ) SEGMENT CREATION IMMEDIATE 
  PCTFREE 10 PCTUSED 40 INITRANS 1 MAXTRANS 255 
 NOCOMPRESS LOGGING
  STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1
  BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT)
  TABLESPACE "USERS" ;

CREATE OR REPLACE EDITIONABLE TRIGGER "DOCLIGHT"."D07_ERROR_LOOKUP_BIU" 
    before insert or update  
    on d07_error_lookup 
    for each row 
begin 
    if inserting then 
        :new.created := sysdate; 
        :new.created_by := coalesce(sys_context('APEX$SESSION','APP_USER'),user); 
    end if; 
    :new.updated := sysdate; 
    :new.updated_by := coalesce(sys_context('APEX$SESSION','APP_USER'),user); 
end d07_error_lookup_biu;

/
ALTER TRIGGER "DOCLIGHT"."D07_ERROR_LOOKUP_BIU" ENABLE;

CREATE UNIQUE INDEX "DOCLIGHT"."D07_ERROR_LOOKUP_ID_PK" ON "DOCLIGHT"."D07_ERROR_LOOKUP" ("ID") 
  PCTFREE 10 INITRANS 2 MAXTRANS 255 COMPUTE STATISTICS 
  STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1
  BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT)
  TABLESPACE "USERS" ;
;

 NOCOMPRESS LOGGING

CREATE OR REPLACE EDITIONABLE TRIGGER "DOCLIGHT"."DEPT_TRG1" 
              before insert on dept
              for each row
              begin
                  if :new.deptno is null then
                      select dept_seq.nextval into :new.deptno from sys.dual;
                 end if;
              end;

/
ALTER TRIGGER "DOCLIGHT"."DEPT_TRG1" ENABLE;

COMMENT ON TABLE DOCLIGHT.DOC_WEB_CON IS 'Contenuti per menu';

COMMENT ON COLUMN DOCLIGHT.DOC_WEB_CON.F_DHTMLX IS 'Flag oggetto in DHTMLX';
COMMENT ON COLUMN DOCLIGHT.DOC_WEB_CON.C_LIN IS 'Lingua';
COMMENT ON COLUMN DOCLIGHT.DOC_WEB_CON.F_JAVA IS 'Flag java';
COMMENT ON COLUMN DOCLIGHT.DOC_WEB_CON.C_TAB IS 'Identificativo TAB (codice linguetta)';
COMMENT ON COLUMN DOCLIGHT.DOC_WEB_CON.F_LNK_EXT IS 'Link esterno';
COMMENT ON COLUMN DOCLIGHT.DOC_WEB_CON.F_OLD IS 'lancio vecchio plsql';
COMMENT ON COLUMN DOCLIGHT.DOC_WEB_CON.N_PAG_ID_APEX IS 'Numero pagina apex';

CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "DOCLIGHT"."DOC_WEB_CON_APEX" ("C_CON", "T_CON", "C_TRG", "T_LNK", "C_TIP", "C_TOO_BAR", "F_DHTMLX", "C_LIN", "F_JAVA", "C_TAB", "F_LNK_EXT", "F_OLD", "N_PAG_ID_APEX", "APPLICATION_ID") AS 
  select "C_CON","T_CON","C_TRG","T_LNK","C_TIP","C_TOO_BAR","F_DHTMLX","C_LIN","F_JAVA","C_TAB","F_LNK_EXT","F_OLD","N_PAG_ID_APEX",application_id
from doc_web_con dwc, APEX_APPLICATION_LIST_ENTRIES le
where dwc.c_con = to_char(le.list_entry_id)
and n_pag_id_apex is not null
AND C_TIP='A'
;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE EDITIONABLE TRIGGER "DOCLIGHT"."BI_DOC_WEB_RUO" 
  before insert or update
  on DOC_WEB_RUO 
  for each row
declare
  -- local variables here
begin
  if :new.f_tip = 'A' then
    :new.c_ruo := upper(:new.c_ruo);
  end if;
end BI_DOC_WEB_RUO;

/
ALTER TRIGGER "DOCLIGHT"."BI_DOC_WEB_RUO" ENABLE;

CREATE INDEX "DOCLIGHT"."TW002_I1" ON "DOCLIGHT"."DOC_WEB_RUO" ("C_SOC", "C_RUO", NVL("F_NON_ATT",'N')) 
  PCTFREE 10 INITRANS 2 MAXTRANS 255 COMPUTE STATISTICS 
  STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1
  BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT)
  TABLESPACE "USERS" ;

CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "DOCLIGHT"."DOC_WEB_SIT_USR_ABI" ("C_SIT", "T_SIT", "T_IMG", "N_POS", "C_SOC", "C_USR") AS 
  select distinct s.c_sit,s.t_sit,s.t_img,s.n_pos,r.c_soc,r.c_usr
    from doc_web_ruo_con c, doc_web_usr_ruo r,doc_web_sit s
   where r.c_ruo = c.c_ruo
     and r.c_soc = c.c_soc
     and c.c_sit = s.c_sit
     and nvl(s.f_abi,'S') = 'S'
;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "DOCLIGHT"."DOC_WEB_SIT_USR_ABI_CON" ("C_SIT", "C_SOC", "C_USR", "C_CON", "N_APP_ID_APEX", "N_PAG_ID_APEX") AS 
  select s.c_sit,r.c_soc,r.c_usr, rc.c_con, s.n_app_id_apex, c.N_PAG_ID_APEX
    from doc_web_ruo_con rc, doc_web_usr_ruo r, doc_web_sit s, doc_web_con_apex c
   where r.c_ruo = rc.c_ruo
     and r.c_soc = rc.c_soc
     and rc.c_sit = s.c_sit
     and c.c_con = rc.c_con
     and nvl(s.f_abi,'S') = 'S'
;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "DOCLIGHT"."DOC_WEB_SIT_USR_ABI_RUO_CON" ("C_SIT", "C_SOC", "C_USR", "C_CON", "N_APP_ID_APEX", "C_RUO", "N_PAG_ID_APEX") AS 
  select s.c_sit,r.c_soc,r.c_usr, rc.c_con, s.n_app_id_apex, r.c_ruo, c.N_PAG_ID_APEX
    from doc_web_ruo_con rc, doc_web_usr_ruo r, doc_web_sit s, doc_web_con_apex c
   where r.c_ruo = rc.c_ruo
     and r.c_soc = rc.c_soc
     and rc.c_sit = s.c_sit
     and c.c_con = rc.c_con
     and nvl(s.f_abi,'S') = 'S'
;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "DOCLIGHT"."DOC_WEB_USR_ARE" ("C_SOC", "C_USR", "C_RUO", "C_ARE", "F_APP") AS 
  select ur.c_soc,ur.c_usr,ra.c_ruo, ra.c_are, ra.f_app
  from td208_ruo_are ra, doc_web_usr_ruo ur
 where ra.c_soc = ur.c_soc
   and ra.c_ruo = ur.c_ruo
;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "DOCLIGHT"."DOC_WEB_USR_RUO_ATT" ("C_SOC", "C_USR", "C_RUO", "T_RUO", "F_TIP") AS 
  select ur.c_soc,ur.c_usr,ur.c_ruo,r.t_ruo,r.f_tip
    from doc_web_ruo r,doc_web_usr_ruo ur
   where ur.c_soc = r.c_soc
     and ur.c_ruo = r.c_ruo
     and nvl(r.f_non_att, 'N') = 'N'
;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE EDITIONABLE TRIGGER "DOCLIGHT"."EMP_TRG1" 
              before insert on emp
              for each row
              begin
                  if :new.empno is null then
                      select emp_seq.nextval into :new.empno from sys.dual;
                 end if;
              end;

/
ALTER TRIGGER "DOCLIGHT"."EMP_TRG1" ENABLE;

  PCTFREE 10 INITRANS 2 MAXTRANS 255 COMPUTE STATISTICS

  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1

CREATE TABLE "DOCLIGHT"."ERROR_LOG" 
   (	"ID_LOG" NUMBER GENERATED BY DEFAULT AS IDENTITY MINVALUE 1 MAXVALUE 9999999999999999999999999999 INCREMENT BY 1 START WITH 1 CACHE 20 NOORDER  NOCYCLE  NOKEEP  NOSCALE  NOT NULL ENABLE, 
	"D_ERR" DATE, 
	"N_ID_APP" NUMBER, 
	"N_ID_PAG" NUMBER, 
	"C_USR" VARCHAR2(100), 
	"T_ERR" CLOB, 
	"ORA_ERR_COD" VARCHAR2(400), 
	"ORA_ERR_MSG" CLOB
   ) SEGMENT CREATION IMMEDIATE 
  PCTFREE 10 PCTUSED 40 INITRANS 1 MAXTRANS 255 
 NOCOMPRESS LOGGING
  STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1
  BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT)
  TABLESPACE "USERS" 
 LOB ("T_ERR") STORE AS SECUREFILE (
  TABLESPACE "USERS" ENABLE STORAGE IN ROW CHUNK 8192
  NOCACHE LOGGING  NOCOMPRESS  KEEP_DUPLICATES 
  STORAGE(INITIAL 106496 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0
  BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT)) 
 LOB ("ORA_ERR_MSG") STORE AS SECUREFILE (
  TABLESPACE "USERS" ENABLE STORAGE IN ROW CHUNK 8192
  NOCACHE LOGGING  NOCOMPRESS  KEEP_DUPLICATES 
  STORAGE(INITIAL 106496 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0
  BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT)) ;

CREATE OR REPLACE EDITIONABLE TRIGGER "DOCLIGHT"."TCS010_BI" 
  before insert on tcs010_idc
  for each row
declare
  -- local variables here
begin
  :new.t_sd_id := :new.c_tip_pac || '_ID_' || :new.n_id_idc;
--  :new.t_desc := :new.c_tip_pac || ' numero ' || :new.n_id_idc || :new.t_desc;
end TCS010_BI;

/
ALTER TRIGGER "DOCLIGHT"."TCS010_BI" ENABLE;
  CREATE OR REPLACE EDITIONABLE TRIGGER "DOCLIGHT"."TCS010_BU" 
  before update on tcs010_idc
  for each row
declare
  -- local variables here
begin
  -- se firma il pda devo controllare che il firmatario sia RespCons e non Creatore PDA per mettere stato approvato
  if :old.c_soc is not null then --and :old.c_soc not in ('A03') then
    if (:new.c_tip_pac='PDA' or :new.c_tip_pac='PDD') and :new.c_sta_idc='F' then
      :new.c_sta_idc:='A';
    end if;
  end if;

  if :old.c_sta_idc='A' then
    -- Posso modificare solo il campo T_ISO e T_ZIP
    if :old.n_id_idc<>:new.n_id_idc or :old.t_url<>:new.t_url or :old.t_ver<>:new.t_ver or :old.t_sd_id<>:new.t_sd_id
      or :old.t_ca_name<>:new.t_ca_name or :old.t_ca_ver<>:new.t_ca_ver or :old.t_ca_prod<>:new.t_ca_prod or :old.n_id_mi_sd<>:new.n_id_mi_sd
      or :old.t_vdc_id<>:new.t_vdc_id or :old.t_vdcgr_lab<>:new.t_vdcgr_lab or :old.t_vdcgr_id<>:new.t_vdcgr_id
      or :old.t_vdcgr_descr<>:new.t_vdcgr_descr or :old.n_id_mi_vdc<>:new.n_id_mi_vdc or :old.t_tr_attach<>:new.t_tr_attach
      or :old.t_tr_detach<>:new.t_tr_detach or :old.t_tr_info<>:new.t_tr_info or :old.t_prc_law<>:new.t_prc_law
      or :old.n_id_mi_prc<>:new.n_id_mi_prc or :old.c_sta_idc<>:new.c_sta_idc
      or :old.d_scad<>:new.d_scad or :old.d_ins<>:new.d_ins or :old.d_cre_xml<>:new.d_cre_xml or :old.t_dir_path<>:new.t_dir_path
      or :old.d_sign_xml<>:new.d_sign_xml or :old.t_desc<>:new.t_desc or :old.c_tip_pac<>:new.c_tip_pac or :old.c_usr<>:new.c_usr
      or :old.t_desc_rif<>:new.t_desc_rif or :old.c_soc<>:new.c_soc or :old.c_usr_app<>:new.c_usr_app
      or :old.d_appr<>:new.d_appr
   then
       RAISE_APPLICATION_ERROR(-20001, 'Pacchetto non modificabile');
    end if;
  end if;


end TCS010_BU;

/
ALTER TRIGGER "DOCLIGHT"."TCS010_BU" ENABLE;

CREATE OR REPLACE EDITIONABLE TRIGGER "DOCLIGHT"."TD000_DOC_ORDS_REST_BI" 
  before insert
  on td000_doc_ords_rest
  for each row
declare
  -- local variables here
begin
  if :NEW.C_DOC is null then
   select TD000_DOC_ORDS_REST_SEQ.nextval into :NEW.C_DOC from sys.dual;
  end if;
end TD000_DOC_ORDS_REST_BI;

/
ALTER TRIGGER "DOCLIGHT"."TD000_DOC_ORDS_REST_BI" ENABLE;

CREATE OR REPLACE EDITIONABLE TRIGGER "DOCLIGHT"."BIUD_TD006" 
  before insert or update of "CD_CAR_PAD" or delete on td006_car
  REFERENCING NEW AS new OLD AS old
  FOR EACH ROW
declare
  -- local variables here
  isPratica number;
begin
  if inserting and :new.cd_car_pad is null then
    --select count(*) into isPratica from td200_pratiche t where t.c_soc = v('PCSOC') and t.c_pra=:new.cd_car; 
    --if isPratica>0 then
    --  insert into td015_rac_mod(cd_rac,fl_adoc,fl_tdoc,fl_pdoc,fl_arpa,cd_soc) values (:new.cd_car,'S','N','S','S',v('PCSOC'));
    --else
      insert into td015_rac_mod(cd_rac,fl_adoc,fl_tdoc,fl_pdoc,fl_arpa,cd_soc) values (:new.cd_car,'S','N','N','S',v('PCSOC'));
    --end if;
  elsif deleting and :old.cd_car_pad is null then
    delete from td015_rac_mod where cd_rac = :old.cd_car and cd_soc=v('PCSOC');
  elsif updating then
    if :old.cd_car_pad is null then
       delete from td015_rac_mod where cd_rac = :old.cd_car and cd_soc=v('PCSOC');
    end if;
    if :new.cd_car_pad is null then
      --select count(*) into isPratica from td200_pratiche t where t.c_soc = v('PCSOC') and t.c_pra=:new.cd_car;  
      --if isPratica>0 then
      --  insert into td015_rac_mod(cd_rac,fl_adoc,fl_tdoc,fl_pdoc,fl_arpa,cd_soc) values (:new.cd_car,'S','N','S','S',v('PCSOC'));
      --else
        insert into td015_rac_mod(cd_rac,fl_adoc,fl_tdoc,fl_pdoc,fl_arpa,cd_soc) values (:new.cd_car,'S','N','N','S',v('PCSOC'));
      --end if;
    end if;
  end if;
end BIUD_TD006;

/
ALTER TRIGGER "DOCLIGHT"."BIUD_TD006" ENABLE;

CREATE OR REPLACE EDITIONABLE TRIGGER "DOCLIGHT"."TD200_TD006" 
  before insert or update or delete on td200_pratiche
  for each row
declare
  VCarPad varchar2(50);
  vGrp    varchar2(10);
  vErr    varchar2(1000);
begin
  if :new.c_soc = 'GE' then
    VCarPad := 'GE_GEIE';
  elsif :new.c_soc = 'XGP' then
    VCarPad := 'PERS';
  elsif :new.c_soc = 'MUS' then
    if substr(:new.c_pra,1,1) >= 5 then
      VCarPad := 'PMUS';
     else
      VCarPad := 'CMUS';
    end if;
  elsif :new.c_soc = 'STF' then
    VCarPad := 'SITAF';
  elsif :new.c_soc = 'SI' then
    VCarPad := 'SI';
  end if;
  
  
  
  if deleting then
      select t.c_grp
        into vGrp
      from td058_grp_soc t
      where t.c_soc = :old.c_soc;

    delete from td006_car t
     where t.cd_car = :old.c_pra;
  elsif inserting then
    begin
      select t.c_grp
        into vGrp
      from td058_grp_soc t
      where t.c_soc = :new.c_soc;
      
      insert into td006_car (cd_car,     ds_car,                  fl_tip, nn_liv, cd_car_pad, c_grp)
                     values (:new.c_pra, substr(:new.t_pra,1,50), 'P',    50,     VCarPad, vGrp);
    exception when others then
      vErr := SUBSTR(SQLERRM, 1, 200);
      --insert into Z_TEST(VC_1) values(vErr);
    end;
  elsif updating then
      select t.c_grp
        into vGrp
      from td058_grp_soc t
      where t.c_soc = :old.c_soc;
      
    if :old.c_pra != :new.c_pra then  
      delete from td006_car t
       where t.cd_car = :old.c_pra;
      --
      insert into td006_car (cd_car,     ds_car,                  fl_tip, nn_liv, cd_car_pad, c_grp)
                     values (:new.c_pra, substr(:new.t_pra,1,50), 'P',    50,     VCarPad, vGrp);
    end if;                 
  end if;
  
end TD200_TD006;

/
ALTER TRIGGER "DOCLIGHT"."TD200_TD006" ENABLE;

  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1

CREATE OR REPLACE EDITIONABLE TRIGGER "DOCLIGHT"."TD201_TD006" 
  before insert or update or delete on td201_sot_pra
  for each row
declare 
  vGrp    varchar2(10);    
begin
  if deleting then
      select t.c_grp
        into vGrp
      from td058_grp_soc t
      where t.c_soc = :old.c_soc;
          
    delete from td006_car t
     where t.cd_car     = :old.c_sot_pra
       and t.cd_car_pad = :old.c_pra
       and t.c_grp = vGrp;
  elsif inserting then
    begin
    select t.c_grp
      into vGrp
      from td058_grp_soc t
     where t.c_soc = :new.c_soc;
   
   insert into td006_car (cd_car,         ds_car,                      fl_tip, nn_liv, cd_car_pad, c_grp)
                   values (:new.c_sot_pra, substr(:new.t_sot_pra,1,50), 'P',    50,     :new.c_pra, vGrp);
    exception when others then
      null;
    end;
  elsif updating('c_usr_resp')  then
    --
      select t.c_grp
        into vGrp
      from td058_grp_soc t
      where t.c_soc = :old.c_soc;
          

    if nvl(:old.c_usr_resp,'$$$') <> nvl(:new.c_usr_resp,'$$$') then
      distribuisci_documenti_pratica(:new.c_soc,:new.c_pra,:new.c_sot_pra,:new.c_usr_resp);
    end if;
    --
    if :old.c_pra <> :new.c_pra or :old.c_sot_pra <> :new.c_sot_pra then
      delete from td006_car t
       where t.cd_car     = :old.c_sot_pra
         and t.cd_car_pad = :old.c_pra
         and t.c_grp = vGrp;
      --
      insert into td006_car (cd_car,         ds_car,                      fl_tip, nn_liv, cd_car_pad, c_grp)
                     values (:new.c_sot_pra, substr(:new.t_sot_pra,1,50), 'P',    50,     :new.c_pra, VGrp);
    end if;
  elsif updating then
      select t.c_grp
        into vGrp
      from td058_grp_soc t
      where t.c_soc = :old.c_soc;
          
    if :old.c_pra <> :new.c_pra or :old.c_sot_pra <> :new.c_sot_pra then
      delete from td006_car t
       where t.cd_car     = :old.c_sot_pra
         and t.cd_car_pad = :old.c_pra;
      --
      insert into td006_car (cd_car,         ds_car,                      fl_tip, nn_liv, cd_car_pad, c_grp)
                     values (:new.c_sot_pra, substr(:new.t_sot_pra,1,50), 'P',    50,     :new.c_pra, VGrp);
    end if;
  end if;
end TD201_TD006;

/

CREATE OR REPLACE EDITIONABLE TRIGGER "DOCLIGHT"."TP003_AID" 
  after insert or delete on tp003_caselle
  for each row
declare

  -- local variables here
begin
  if inserting then
    insert into TP013_SRV_CAS (C_ID_CAS, T_SRV, N_TRD)
    values (:new.c_id_cas, 'bfiler', :new.c_id_cas);
  else
    delete from tp013_srv_cas where c_id_cas = :old.c_id_cas;
  end if;
end TP003_AID;

/
ALTER TRIGGER "DOCLIGHT"."TP003_AID" ENABLE;

  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1
  BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT)
  TABLESPACE "USERS" ;

   ) SEGMENT CREATION IMMEDIATE

CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "DOCLIGHT"."USER_MOST_VIEWED" ("CLICKS", "PAGE_ID", "PAGE_NAME") AS 
  select count(*) clicks, page_id, page_name
 from APEX_WORKSPACE_ACTIVITY_LOG
where application_id= nvl(v('APP_ID'), 200)
and view_date>(sysdate-30)
and page_view_type='Rendering'
and APEX_USER = nvl(v('PCUSR'), 'Admin')
and page_id!=1 -- levo la home
group by page_id, page_name
;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "DOCLIGHT"."VCARDS" ("ID_PAG", "PARENT_ENTRY_TEXT", "LIST_TITLE", "ENTRY_TARGET", "C4_IS_CURRENT", "ICON_CLASS", "C7_ICON_ALT_TEXT", "DISPLAY_SEQUENCE", "ENTRY_TEXT", "LIST_NAME") AS 
  select apex_tema_abi.getPagFromUrl(pEntryTarget => le.entry_target) id_pag,
       le.parent_entry_text,
       le.entry_text   list_title,
       le.entry_target,
       /*APEX_TEMA_UTL.apex_url_facility_direct(pPage        => apex_tema_abi.getPagFromUrl(pEntryTarget => le.entry_target),
                                              pField              => 'P90_PARENT,P90_TITOLO',
                                              pValue              => substr(le.entry_target, instr(le.entry_target,':',1,7)+1, instr(le.entry_target,':',1,8)-instr(le.entry_target,':',1,7)-1),
                                              pApplicationProcess => null)  link,*/
       'YES'             c4_is_current,
       'fa '||le.entry_image   icon_class,
       le.entry_text      c7_icon_alt_text,
       le.display_sequence,
       le.entry_text,
       le.list_name
      from APEX_APPLICATION_LIST_ENTRIES le
      where  le.application_id = nvl(v('APP_ID'), 200)
       and le.list_name='Desktop Navigation Menu'
       --and (:P90_PARENT is null or le.parent_entry_text=:P90_PARENT)
       /*and (APEX_TEMA_ABI.canSeeMenuNode(pNode=>le.entry_text)=TRUE
            or  APEX_TEMA_ABI.canSeePage(pPageId => apex_tema_abi.getPagFromUrl(pEntryTarget => le.entry_target))=TRUE
       )
       */
       order by le.display_sequence
;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "DOCLIGHT"."VCS052_MD_CD_DOC_INF" ("N_ORD_MD", "C_GRP", "C_SUB_GRP", "T_ALS_COL_50", "F_ATT", "F_OBB", "C_TIP", "F_MUL", "F_DEF", "C_GRP_DOC_INF", "C_SUB_GRP_DOC_INF", "T_ALS_COL", "C_SOC", "C_TIP_TF", "T_TAB_SRC", "T_COL_SRC", "T_KEY_TF", "COL", "ASTERISCO") AS 
  select t50.n_ord_md,
       t50.c_grp,
       t50.c_sub_grp,
       --t50.t_als_col t_als_col_50,
       decode(instr(t52.c_grp_doc_inf, '#'),0, t50.t_als_col,t52.c_grp_doc_inf || '.' || T52.C_SUB_GRP_DOC_INF) t_als_col_50,
       t50.f_att,
       t50.f_obb,
       t50.c_tip,
       t50.f_mul,
       t52.f_def,
       t52.c_grp_doc_inf,
       T52.C_SUB_GRP_DOC_INF,
       t52.c_grp_doc_inf || '.' || T52.C_SUB_GRP_DOC_INF as t_als_col,
       t52.c_soc,
       t52.c_tip_tf,
       t52.t_tab_src,
       t52.t_col_src,
       t52.t_key_tf,
       'col' || lpad(rownum, 2, '0') col,
       decode(t50.f_obb, 'S', '*', '') asterisco
       --, CS0007_KEY.isModificabileChiaviObb(decode(instr(t52.c_grp_doc_inf, '#'),0, t50.t_als_col,t52.c_grp_doc_inf || '.' || T52.C_SUB_GRP_DOC_INF), t52.c_soc, t52.c_tip_tf) modificabile
  from TCS050_MD_DOC_INF t50, TCS052_MD_CD_DOC_INF t52
 where t50.c_grp =
       substr(t52.c_grp_doc_inf,
              1,
              decode(instr(t52.c_grp_doc_inf, '#'),
                     0,
                     length(t52.c_grp_doc_inf),
                     instr(t52.c_grp_doc_inf, '#') - 1))
   and t50.c_sub_grp = t52.c_sub_grp_doc_inf
      --and t52.t_tab_src='TD003_DOC_KEY'
   and nvl(t50.f_att, 'S') = 'S'
 order by 1, 2
;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "DOCLIGHT"."VCS052_MD_CD_DOC_INF_DEF" ("N_ORD_MD", "C_GRP", "C_SUB_GRP", "T_ALS_COL_50", "F_ATT", "F_OBB", "C_TIP", "F_MUL", "F_DEF", "C_GRP_DOC_INF", "C_SUB_GRP_DOC_INF", "T_ALS_COL", "C_SOC", "C_TIP_TF", "T_TAB_SRC", "T_COL_SRC", "T_KEY_TF", "COL", "ASTERISCO", "MODIFICABILE") AS 
  select t50.n_ord_md,
       t50.c_grp,
       t50.c_sub_grp,
       --t50.t_als_col t_als_col_50,
       decode(t52.c_grp_doc_inf, null, t50.t_als_col, (decode(instr(t52.c_grp_doc_inf, '#'),0, t50.t_als_col,t52.c_grp_doc_inf || '.' || T52.C_SUB_GRP_DOC_INF))) t_als_col_50,
       t50.f_att,
       t50.f_obb,
       t50.c_tip,
       t50.f_mul,
       t52.f_def,
       nvl(t52.c_grp_doc_inf, t50.c_grp) c_grp_doc_inf,
       nvl(T52.C_SUB_GRP_DOC_INF, t50.c_sub_grp) C_SUB_GRP_DOC_INF,
       t52.c_grp_doc_inf || '.' || T52.C_SUB_GRP_DOC_INF as t_als_col,
       t52.c_soc,
       t52.c_tip_tf,
       t52.t_tab_src,
       t52.t_col_src,
       t52.t_key_tf,
       'col' || lpad(rownum, 2, '0') col,
       decode(t50.f_obb, 'S', '*', '') asterisco
       , CS0007_KEY.isModificabileChiaviObb(decode(instr(t52.c_grp_doc_inf, '#'),0, t50.t_als_col,t52.c_grp_doc_inf || '.' || T52.C_SUB_GRP_DOC_INF), t52.c_soc, t52.c_tip_tf) modificabile
  from TCS050_MD_DOC_INF t50 left join TCS052_MD_CD_DOC_INF t52
    on t50.c_sub_grp = t52.c_sub_grp_doc_inf
    and t50.c_grp =
       substr(t52.c_grp_doc_inf,
              1,
              decode(instr(t52.c_grp_doc_inf, '#'),
                     0,
                     length(t52.c_grp_doc_inf),
                     instr(t52.c_grp_doc_inf, '#') - 1))
 where nvl(t50.f_att, 'S') = 'S'
 order by 1, 2
;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "DOCLIGHT"."VD001_UTE_RUO" ("CD_SOC", "CD_USR", "CD_RUO") AS 
  select c_soc cd_soc,
          c_usr cd_usr,
          c_ruo cd_ruo
     from doc_web_usr_ruo
;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "DOCLIGHT"."VD006_CAR_TREE" ("LEVEL", "CD_CAR", "DS_CAR", "CD_CAR_PAD", "CD_CAR_ROOT", "DS_CAR_ROOT") AS 
  select "LEVEL",CD_CAR,DS_CAR,CD_CAR_PAD,CD_CAR_ROOT,DS_CAR_ROOT
from (SELECT LEVEL, /*LPAD (' ', 2 * (LEVEL - 1)) ||*/  cd_car, ds_car, cd_car_pad,
CONNECT_BY_ROOT cd_car "CD_CAR_ROOT",
CONNECT_BY_ROOT ds_car "DS_CAR_ROOT"
FROM TD006_CAR START WITH cd_car_pad IS NULL
CONNECT BY PRIOR cd_car = cd_car_pad
ORDER SIBLINGS BY ds_car ASC) t
;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "DOCLIGHT"."VD007_DES_MIT" ("C_SOC", "C_SOG", "T_SOG", "C_TIP_SOG") AS 
  SELECT C_SOC, c_sog_int c_SOG, T_sog_int T_SOG, 'I' C_TIP_SOG
FROM td030_des_int
UNION
select C_SOC, c_sog_est SOG, T_sog_EST T_SOG, 'E' C_TIP_SOG
from td031_des_est
;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "DOCLIGHT"."VD058_GRP_SOC" ("C_SOC", "T_SOC", "C_COD_IVA", "D_INI", "C_LIV", "N_GG_PWD_DEF", "C_COD_FIS", "C_SOC_TOPFILER", "C_GRP") AS 
  select d.c_soc,
         d.t_soc,
         d.c_cod_iva,
         d.d_ini,
         d.c_liv,
         d.n_gg_pwd_def,
         d.c_cod_fis,
         d.c_soc_topfiler,
         t.c_grp
    from TD058_GRP_SOC t, DOC_WEB_SOC d
   where t.c_soc = d.c_soc
;

CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "DOCLIGHT"."VD201_PRA_SOT_PRA" ("C_SOC", "C_FIG", "C_PAD", "T_PRA", "FIGLI", "LIV", "C_USR_RESP") AS 
  select t200.c_soc, t200.c_pra c_fig, null c_pad, t200.t_pra, count_sotto_pratiche(pcSoc=>t200.c_soc, pcPadre=>c_pra) figli, 0 liv, t200.c_usr_resp
from td200_pratiche t200
union
select t201.c_soc, t201.c_sot_pra, t201.c_pra, t201.t_sot_pra, count_sotto_pratiche(pcSoc=>t201.c_soc, pcPadre=>c_sot_pra) figli, 1 liv, t201.c_usr_resp
from td200_pratiche t200, td201_sot_pra t201
where t201.c_pra = t200.c_pra
  and t201.c_soc = t200.c_soc
union
select t201f.c_soc, t201f.c_sot_pra, t201f.c_pra, t201f.t_sot_pra, count_sotto_pratiche(pcSoc=>t201f.c_soc, pcPadre=>t201f.c_sot_pra) figli, 1 liv, t201f.c_usr_resp
from td201_sot_pra t201p, td201_sot_pra t201f
where t201p.c_sot_pra = t201f.c_pra
  and t201p.c_soc = t201f.c_soc
;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "DOCLIGHT"."VWF_DOC_TASKS" ("ID", "C_USR", "STATUS", "DECISION_DATE", "APPROVER", "APPROVAL_TASK_ID", "WORKFLOW_ID", "CD_DOC", "NEED_BY", "REQUEST_DATE", "CD_SOC", "TASK_ID", "WORKSPACE_ID", "WORKSPACE", "WORKSPACE_DISPLAY_NAME", "APPLICATION_ID", "APPLICATION_NAME", "WORKING_COPY_NAME", "TASK_DEF_ID", "TASK_DEF_NAME", "TASK_DEF_STATIC_ID", "PREVIOUS_TASK_ID", "SUBJECT", "TASK_TYPE_CODE", "TASK_TYPE", "DUE_ON", "PRIORITY", "PRIORITY_LEVEL", "DETAIL_PK", "INITIATOR", "INITIATOR_CAN_COMPLETE", "ACTUAL_OWNER", "PREVIOUS_OWNER", "STATE_CODE", "STATE", "RENEWAL_COUNT", "OUTCOME_CODE", "OUTCOME", "CREATED_BY", "CREATED_ON", "LAST_UPDATED_BY", "LAST_UPDATED_ON", "NEXT_APPR") AS 
  select
       wf.id,
       wf.c_usr,
       wf.status,
       wf.decision_date,
       wf.approver,
       wf.approval_task_id,
       wf.workflow_id,
       wf.cd_doc,
       wf.need_by,
       wf.request_date,
       wf.cd_soc,
       t.task_id,
       t.workspace_id,
       t.workspace,
       t.workspace_display_name,
       t.application_id,
       t.application_name,
       t.working_copy_name,
       t.task_def_id,
       t.task_def_name,
       t.task_def_static_id,
       t.previous_task_id,
       t.subject,
       t.task_type_code,
       t.task_type,
       t.due_on,
       t.priority,
       t.priority_level,
       t.detail_pk,
       t.initiator,
       t.initiator_can_complete,
       t.actual_owner,
       t.previous_owner,
       t.state_code,
       t.state,
       t.renewal_count,
       t.outcome_code,
       t.outcome,
       t.created_by,
       t.created_on,
       t.last_updated_by,
       t.last_updated_on,
       wf_approvals.lista_approvatori_documento(wf.cd_doc) next_appr

from apex_Tasks t, WF_DOC_APPR_REQUEST wf, td001_doc_det t1
where t.application_id=nvl(nv('APP_ID'), 200)
and wf.id = t.detail_pk
and wf.cd_doc = t1.cd_doc
and wf.cd_soc = t1.cd_soc
and t1.cd_soc = nvl(v('PCSOC'), 'A03')
order by t.detail_pk desc
;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "DOCLIGHT"."VWF_DOC_TASKS_LAST" ("ID", "C_USR", "STATUS", "DECISION_DATE", "APPROVER", "APPROVAL_TASK_ID", "WORKFLOW_ID", "CD_DOC", "NEED_BY", "REQUEST_DATE", "CD_SOC", "TASK_ID", "WORKSPACE_ID", "WORKSPACE", "WORKSPACE_DISPLAY_NAME", "APPLICATION_ID", "APPLICATION_NAME", "WORKING_COPY_NAME", "TASK_DEF_ID", "TASK_DEF_NAME", "TASK_DEF_STATIC_ID", "PREVIOUS_TASK_ID", "SUBJECT", "TASK_TYPE_CODE", "TASK_TYPE", "DUE_ON", "PRIORITY", "PRIORITY_LEVEL", "DETAIL_PK", "INITIATOR", "INITIATOR_CAN_COMPLETE", "ACTUAL_OWNER", "PREVIOUS_OWNER", "STATE_CODE", "STATE", "RENEWAL_COUNT", "OUTCOME_CODE", "OUTCOME", "CREATED_BY", "CREATED_ON", "LAST_UPDATED_BY", "LAST_UPDATED_ON", "NEXT_APPR") AS 
  select
       wf.id,
       wf.c_usr,
       wf.status,
       wf.decision_date,
       wf.approver,
       wf.approval_task_id,
       wf.workflow_id,
       wf.cd_doc,
       wf.need_by,
       wf.request_date,
       wf.cd_soc,
       t.task_id,
       t.workspace_id,
       t.workspace,
       t.workspace_display_name,
       t.application_id,
       t.application_name,
       t.working_copy_name,
       t.task_def_id,
       t.task_def_name,
       t.task_def_static_id,
       t.previous_task_id,
       t.subject,
       t.task_type_code,
       t.task_type,
       t.due_on,
       t.priority,
       t.priority_level,
       t.detail_pk,
       t.initiator,
       t.initiator_can_complete,
       t.actual_owner,
       t.previous_owner,
       t.state_code,
       t.state,
       t.renewal_count,
       t.outcome_code,
       t.outcome,
       t.created_by,
       t.created_on,
       t.last_updated_by,
       t.last_updated_on,
       wf_approvals.lista_approvatori_documento(wf.cd_doc) next_appr

from (select ti.* from apex_Tasks ti
       where ti.last_updated_on = (select max(last_updated_on) from apex_Tasks maxAt where ti.workflow_id = maxAt.workflow_id)) t, WF_DOC_APPR_REQUEST wf, td001_doc_det t1
where t.application_id=nvl(nv('APP_ID'), 200)
and wf.id = t.detail_pk
and wf.cd_doc = t1.cd_doc
and wf.cd_soc = t1.cd_soc
and t1.cd_soc = nvl(v('PCSOC'), 'A03')
order by t.detail_pk desc
;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "DOCLIGHT"."VWF_DOC_WFLOWS" ("ID", "C_USR", "STATUS", "DECISION_DATE", "APPROVER", "APPROVAL_TASK_ID", "WORKFLOW_ID", "CD_DOC", "NEED_BY", "REQUEST_DATE", "CD_SOC", "APPLICATION_ID", "TITLE", "WORKFLOW_DEF_NAME", "DETAIL_PK", "INITIATOR", "STATE_CODE", "STATE", "START_TIME", "END_TIME", "IS_DEV_MODE", "LAST_UPDATED_BY", "LAST_UPDATED_ON") AS 
  select r.id,
       r.c_usr,
       r.status,
       r.decision_date,
       r.approver,
       r.approval_task_id,
       r.workflow_id,
       r.cd_doc,
       r.need_by,
       r.request_date,
       r.cd_soc,
       t.application_id,
       t.title,
       t.workflow_def_name,
       /*
       t.workflow_id,
       t.workspace_id,
       t.workspace,
       t.workspace_display_name,
       t.application_id,
       t.application_name,
       t.workflow_def_id,
       t.workflow_def_static_id,
       t.workflow_version_id,
       t.workflow_version,
       t.workflow_version_state,
       */t.detail_pk,
       t.initiator,
       t.state_code,
       t.state,
       t.start_time,
       t.end_time,

;

CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "DOCLIGHT"."VWF_DOC_WF_STATUS" ("ID", "C_USR", "STATUS", "STATUS_ITA", "DECISION_DATE", "APPROVER", "WORKFLOW_ID", "CD_DOC", "REQUEST_DATE", "APPLICATION_ID", "TITLE", "WORKFLOW_DEF_NAME", "INITIATOR_WF", "STATE_CODE_WF", "STATE_WF", "START_TIME", "END_TIME", "TASK_DEF_NAME", "SUBJECT", "DETAIL_PK", "INITIATOR_TASK", "ACTUAL_OWNER", "PREVIOUS_OWNER", "STATE_CODE_TASK", "STATE_TASK", "OUTCOME_CODE", "OUTCOME", "CREATED_BY", "CREATED_ON", "LAST_UPDATED_BY", "LAST_UPDATED_ON") AS 
  select r.id,
       r.c_usr,
       r.status,
       decode(r.status,
          'PENDING', 'IN ATTESA',
          'REJECTED', 'RIFIUTATO',
          'APPROVED', 'APPROVATO',
          r.status
       ) status_ita,
       r.decision_date,
       r.approver,
       --r.approval_task_id,
       r.workflow_id,
       r.cd_doc,
       --r.need_by,
       r.request_date,
       --r.cd_soc,
       t.application_id,
       t.title,
       t.workflow_def_name,
       --t.detail_pk,
       t.initiator initiator_wf,
       t.state_code state_code_wf,
       t.state state_wf,
       t.start_time,
       t.end_time,
       --t.is_dev_mode,
       --t.last_updated_by,
       --t.last_updated_on,
       --x.task_id,
       --x.workspace_id,
       --x.workspace,
       --x.workspace_display_name,
       --x.application_id,
       --x.application_name,
       --x.working_copy_name,
       --x.task_def_id,
       x.task_def_name,
       --x.task_def_static_id,
       --x.previous_task_id,
       x.subject,
       --x.task_type_code,
       --x.task_type,
       --x.due_on,
       --x.priority,
       --x.priority_level,
       x.detail_pk,
       x.initiator initiator_task,
       x.actual_owner,
       x.previous_owner,
       x.state_code state_code_task,
       x.state state_task,
      -- x.renewal_count,
       x.outcome_code,
       x.outcome,
       x.created_by,
       x.created_on,
       x.last_updated_by,
       x.last_updated_on

from apex_workflows t inner join WF_DOC_APPR_REQUEST r
on t.workflow_id = r.workflow_id
inner join td001_doc_det t1 on r.cd_doc = t1.cd_doc
--left outer join apex_tasks x on r.workflow_id=t.workflow_id
right outer join apex_tasks x on r.workflow_id=t.workflow_id
and r.id = x.detail_pk
where t.application_id=nvl(nv('APP_ID'), 200)
and t1.cd_soc = r.cd_soc
and t1.cd_soc = nvl(v('PCSOC'), 'A03')

--and r.status <> 'NOT_NEEDED'
;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "DOCLIGHT"."VWF_TASK_BADGE" ("TITLE", "SUBTITLE", "BODY", "SECONDARY_BODY", "BODY_CLASS", "STATE_CODE", "INITIATOR", "ACTUAL_OWNER", "CREATED_ON", "CD_SOC", "TASK_ID", "CD_DOC", "DUE_ON", "APPROVER", "APPLICATION_ID", "NEXT_APPR") AS 
  select t.subject title,
       'Richiesta il '||to_char(t.request_date, 'dd/mm/rrrr')||' by '||WF_APPROVALS.getPersonName(t.initiator) subtitle,
       WF_APPROVALS.getChiaviDocumento(pcDoc => t.cd_doc) body,

       case t.state_code
            when 'UNASSIGNED' then 'UNASSIGNED'
            when 'ASSIGNED' then t.status||' - Assigned to '||WF_APPROVALS.getPersonName(t.actual_owner)||' - Due on '||to_char(t.due_on, 'dd/mm/rrrr')
            when 'COMPLETED' then
                case t.outcome_code
                    when 'REJECTED' then '<font style="color:red">REJECTED</font> by '||WF_APPROVALS.getPersonName(t.approver)||' on '||to_char(t.decision_date, 'dd/mm/rrrr')
                    when 'APPROVED' then 'APPROVED by '||WF_APPROVALS.getPersonName(t.approver)||' on '||to_char(t.decision_date, 'dd/mm/rrrr')
                    else 'NO OUTCOME CODE'
                end
            else t.state_code
        end as secondary_body,

       case t.state_code
            when 'COMPLETED' then
                case t.outcome_code
                    when 'REJECTED' then 'u-danger-text'
                    when 'APPROVED' then 'u-success-text'
                    else ''
                end
            else ''
        end as BODY_CLASS,

        t.STATE_CODE,
        t.initiator,
        t.actual_owner,
        t.created_on,
        t.cd_soc,
        t.TASK_ID,
        cd_doc,
        t.due_on,
        t.approver,
        application_id,
        t.next_appr

from VWF_DOC_TASKS t
where application_id=nvl(nv('APP_ID'),200)
and t.cd_soc = nvl(v('PCSOC'), 'A03')
;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "DOCLIGHT"."VWF_TASK_BADGE_LAST" ("TITLE", "SUBTITLE", "BODY", "SECONDARY_BODY", "BODY_CLASS", "STATE_CODE", "INITIATOR", "ACTUAL_OWNER", "CREATED_ON", "CD_SOC", "TASK_ID", "CD_DOC", "DUE_ON", "APPROVER", "APPLICATION_ID", "NEXT_APPR") AS 
  select t.subject title,
       'Richiesta il '||to_char(t.request_date, 'dd/mm/rrrr')||' by '||WF_APPROVALS.getPersonName(t.initiator) subtitle,
       WF_APPROVALS.getChiaviDocumento(pcDoc => t.cd_doc) body,

       case t.state_code
            when 'UNASSIGNED' then 'UNASSIGNED'
            when 'ASSIGNED' then t.status||' - Assigned to '||WF_APPROVALS.getPersonName(t.actual_owner)||' - Due on '||to_char(t.due_on, 'dd/mm/rrrr')
            when 'COMPLETED' then
                case t.outcome_code
                    when 'REJECTED' then '<font style="color:red">REJECTED</font> by '||WF_APPROVALS.getPersonName(t.approver)||' on '||to_char(t.decision_date, 'dd/mm/rrrr')
                    when 'APPROVED' then 'APPROVED by '||WF_APPROVALS.getPersonName(t.approver)||' on '||to_char(t.decision_date, 'dd/mm/rrrr')
                    else 'NO OUTCOME CODE'
                end
            else t.state_code
        end as secondary_body,

       case t.state_code
            when 'COMPLETED' then
                case t.outcome_code
                    when 'REJECTED' then 'u-danger-text'
                    when 'APPROVED' then 'u-success-text'
                    else ''
                end
            else ''
        end as BODY_CLASS,

        t.STATE_CODE,
        t.initiator,
        t.actual_owner,
        t.created_on,
        t.cd_soc,
        t.TASK_ID,
        cd_doc,
        t.due_on,
        t.approver,
        application_id,
        t.next_appr

from VWF_DOC_TASKS_last t
where application_id=nvl(nv('APP_ID'),200)
and t.cd_soc = nvl(v('PCSOC'), 'A03')
;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "DOCLIGHT"."VWF_WORKFLOW_BADGE" ("WORKFLOW_ID", "TITLE", "INITIATOR_WF", "REQUEST_DATE", "BADGE_TEXT", "WORKFLOW_DEF_NAME", "STATE_CODE", "BADGE_BODY", "BADGE_STATE", "BADGE_VALUE", "APPLICATION_ID", "CD_DOC") AS 
  select distinct workflow_id,
       title,
       initiator_wf,
       request_date,
       subject badge_text,
       workflow_def_name,
       state_code_wf state_code,
       'Request on '||to_char(request_date, 'dd/mm/rrrr HH24:mi')||' by '||WF_APPROVALS.getPersonName(initiator_wf) badge_body,
        case state_code_wf
         when 'COMPLETED' then
              case status
                when 'REJECTED' then 'danger'
                when 'APPROVED'  then 'success'
                else 'info'
         end
         when 'TERMINATED' then 'info'
         when 'FAULTED'    then 'danger'
         when 'ACTIVE' then 'warning'

         else 'info'
       end as BADGE_STATE,

        case state_code_WF
         when 'COMPLETED' then
              case status
                when 'REJECTED' then 'RIFIUTATO'
                when 'APPROVED'  then 'APPROVATO'
                else 'NO_EXIT'
         end
         when 'TERMINATED' then 'TERMINATO'
         when 'FAULTED'    then 'FALLITO'
         when 'ACTIVE' then 'ATTIVO'
         else 'NESSUNO STATO'
       end as BADGE_VALUE,
       application_id,

       cd_doc
  from vwf_doc_wf_status t
  where application_id = nvl(nv('APP_ID'),200)
    and status <> 'NOT_NEEDED'
  order by request_date desc nulls last
;
;

 NOCOMPRESS LOGGING

COMMENT ON COLUMN DOCLIGHT.WF_DOC_APPR_APPROVERS.N_STEP IS 'Step di approvazione';
COMMENT ON COLUMN DOCLIGHT.WF_DOC_APPR_APPROVERS.C_ACT_ON_ASSIGN IS 'Azione da fare in caso di assegnazione del task (M=send mail, P=push notification, M:P=entrambi)';

CREATE OR REPLACE procedure DOCLIGHT.ab_tst_sub is
  vDocName varchar2(100);
begin
  genpdf.Init;
  genpdf.NewPage;
  genpdf.PrintText (50, 50, 'Abcd<sub>ef</sub> ghij');
  genpdf.CreateDocument('T', vDocName);
  dbms_output.put_line(vDocName);
end ab_tst_sub;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.accent_replace(str in varchar2) return varchar2  is
  VRet varchar2(32000) ;
begin
  VRet := str;
  VRet := replace(VRet,'&','&amp;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'à','&agrave;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'è','&egrave;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'é','&eacute;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'ì','&igrave;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'ò','&ograve;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'ù','&ugrave;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'À','&Agrave;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'È','&Egrave;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'É','&Eacute;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ì','&Igrave;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ò','&Ograve;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ù','&Ugrave;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Á','&Aacute;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'É','&Eacute;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Í','&Iacute;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ó','&Oacute;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ú','&Uacute;');
  --
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Â','&Aring;');
  VRet := replace(Vret,'Ã','&Atilde;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'§','&sect;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'ª','&ordf;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Å','&Acirc;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ä','&Auml;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Æ','&AElig;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ç','&Ccedil;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ê','&Ecirc;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ë','&Euml;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Î','&Icirc;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ï','&Iuml;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ñ','&Ntilde;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ô','&Ocirc;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Õ','&Otilde;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ö','&Ouml;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Û','&Ucirc;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ü','&Uuml;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ø','&Oslash;');
  --VRet := replace(VRet,'''','''');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'°','&deg;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'>','&gt;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'<','&lt;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'¿','&euro;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'¿',' ');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'¿','''');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'¿','"');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'¿','"');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'¿','-');
  VRet := replace(VRet,' ',' ');
  return(VRet);
end accent_replace;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.accent_replace_clob(str in clob) return clob  is
  VRet clob ;
begin
  VRet := str;
  VRet := replace(VRet,'&','&amp;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'à','&agrave;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'è','&egrave;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'é','&eacute;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'ì','&igrave;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'ò','&ograve;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'ù','&ugrave;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'À','&Agrave;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'È','&Egrave;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'É','&Eacute;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ì','&Igrave;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ò','&Ograve;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ù','&Ugrave;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Á','&Aacute;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'É','&Eacute;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Í','&Iacute;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ó','&Oacute;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ú','&Uacute;');
  --
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Â','&Aring;');
  VRet := replace(Vret,'Ã','&Atilde;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'§','&sect;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'ª','&ordf;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Å','&Acirc;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ä','&Auml;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Æ','&AElig;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ç','&Ccedil;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ê','&Ecirc;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ë','&Euml;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Î','&Icirc;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ï','&Iuml;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ñ','&Ntilde;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ô','&Ocirc;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Õ','&Otilde;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ö','&Ouml;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Û','&Ucirc;');

  --VRet := replace(VRet,'''','''');

  VRet := replace(VRet,'>','&gt;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'<','&lt;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'¿','&euro;');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'¿',' ');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'¿','''');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'¿','"');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'¿','"');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'¿','-');
  VRet := replace(VRet,' ',' ');
  return(VRet);
end accent_replace_clob;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.appartiene_gruppo(pCSoc in varchar2, pcGrp in varchar2) return varchar2 is
  cnt  number;
begin
  select count(*) 
    into cnt
    from td058_grp_soc t58 
   where t58.c_grp = pcGrp 
     and t58.c_soc = pCSoc;
  
  if cnt>0 then return 'Y'; else return 'N'; end if;
end appartiene_gruppo;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE procedure DOCLIGHT.auto_compose(PCIds in varchar2, pSep in varchar2) is
    VTmpDoc  TD000_TMP_DOC%Rowtype;
    Usr      varchar2(200);
    NewDocName varchar2(400);
    vGenpfdInitDone varchar2(1) := 'N';
    PDocName  varchar2(400);

    cursor documenti is
      select t.c_id, t.t_blob, t.c_usr_id, t.doc_size, t.t_ext, t.d_load, t.t_mime
        from td000_tmp_doc t, table(apex_string.split(PCIds, pSep)) sel
       where sel.column_value = t.c_id
       order by t.n_ord_cmp, c_id;


  procedure drawImage(image in blob, imageW in number, imageH in number, areaW in number, areaH in number, x in number, y in number) is
    nRatioW   number;
    nRatioH   number;
    nRatio    number;
    w         number;
    h         number;
    xcenter   number;
  begin
        nRatioW := imageW/areaW;
        if areaH = 0 then
           nRatioH := 0;
        else
           nRatioH := imageH/areaH;
        end if;
        if nRatioW >= nRatioH then
          nRatio := nRatioW;
        else
          nRatio := nRatioH;
        end if;

       w := imageW;
       h := imageH;

       if nRatio>1 then
         w := imageW/nRatio;
         h := imageH/nRatio;
       end if;

       xcenter := x + areaW/2-w/2;

       genpdf.DrawImage(image, xcenter+1, y+1, w, h);

  end drawImage;

  
begin
  apex_debug.message('PCIds='||PCIds);
  begin
      for d in documenti loop
        htp.prn('elabora '||d.c_id);
        if isEan13(d.c_id)='S' then -- è un ean
          htp.prn('isEan13 true');
          if vGenpfdInitDone='N' then  -- è il promo ean
            htp.prn('è il primo ean');
            select substr(d.c_id, 1, decode(instr(d.c_id, '.', -1), 0, length(d.c_id), instr(d.c_id, '.', -1)-1))
              into NewDocName
              from dual;
            htp.prn('inizializzo nuovo pdf => '||NewDocName);  
            genpdf.init('A4', 'P');
            vGenpfdInitDone:='S';
            genpdf.setmargin(1,1,1,1);
            genpdf.SetFillColor(215,215,215);
            genpdf.SetFont('Arial',null,8);

            genpdf.NewPage;
            select * 
              into VTmpDoc
              from td000_tmp_doc
             where c_id = d.c_id;
            htp.prn('Aggiungo immagine al file');
            drawImage(VTmpDoc.t_Blob, 208, 295, 208, 295, 0, 0);

            delete from td000_tmp_doc
             where c_id = d.c_id;
           else -- non è il primo ean
              htp.prn('non è il primo ean');
              Usr:=VTmpDoc.c_Usr_Id;
              genpdf.CreateDocument('T',   PDocName);
              htp.prn('creo pdf => '||PDocName);  
              insert into td000_tmp_doc (c_id, t_blob, c_usr_id, doc_size, f_cmp, t_ext, f_Zebra_Prot, d_load, t_mime)
              (select NewDocName||'.pdf', blob_file, Usr, 1, 'S', 'pdf', VTmpDoc.f_Zebra_Prot, sysdate, 'application/pdf' from genpdf_store_blob where cdoc=PDocName);
               htp.prn('inserisco pdf => '||NewDocName||'.pdf');
                 
             -- inizializzo il nuovo documento
            select substr(d.c_id, 1, decode(instr(d.c_id, '.', -1), 0, length(d.c_id), instr(d.c_id, '.', -1)-1))
              into NewDocName
              from dual;

              htp.prn('inizializzo nuovo pdf => '||NewDocName);  
              
              genpdf.init('A4', 'P');
              vGenpfdInitDone:='S';
              genpdf.setmargin(1,1,1,1);
              genpdf.SetFillColor(215,215,215);
              genpdf.SetFont('Arial',null,8);

              genpdf.NewPage;
              select * 
                into VTmpDoc
                from td000_tmp_doc
               where c_id = d.c_id;

              htp.prn('Aggiungo immagine al file');
              drawImage(VTmpDoc.t_Blob, 208, 295, 208, 295, 0, 0);

              delete from td000_tmp_doc
               where c_id = d.c_id;
           end if;
        else -- non è un ean
          htp.prn('isEan13 not true');
          if vGenpfdInitDone='N' then -- non ci sono ean precedenti a questo documento
            htp.prn('non ci sono ean precedenti a questo documento');
            null; -- non faccio nulla sul documanto
          else -- c'è un ean precedente a questo documento
            htp.prn('c''è un ean precedente a questo documento');
            genpdf.NewPage;
            select * 
              into VTmpDoc
              from td000_tmp_doc
             where c_id = d.c_id;

            htp.prn('Aggiungo immagine al file');
            drawImage(VTmpDoc.t_Blob, 208, 295, 208, 295, 0, 0);

            delete from td000_tmp_doc
             where c_id = d.c_id;
          end if;
        end if;    
        
      end loop;

      if vGenpfdInitDone='N' then -- non ci sono mai stati ean
        htp.prn('nessun documento con ean');
        null;
      else
        Usr:=VTmpDoc.c_Usr_Id;
        genpdf.CreateDocument('T',   PDocName);
        htp.prn('creo pdf => '||PDocName);      
        insert into td000_tmp_doc (c_id, t_blob, c_usr_id, doc_size, f_cmp, t_ext, f_Zebra_Prot, d_load, t_mime)
        (select NewDocName||'.pdf', blob_file, Usr, dbms_lob.getlength(blob_file), 'S', 'pdf', VTmpDoc.f_Zebra_Prot, sysdate, 'application/pdf' from genpdf_store_blob where cdoc=PDocName);
        htp.prn('inserisco pdf => '||NewDocName||'.pdf');
      end if;

   exception when others then
     dbms_output.put_line(sqlerrM);
   end;      
end auto_compose;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.BFileHash(pOracleDir in varchar2, pFilename in varchar2) return raw is
  -- Returns the hash of a file, which can be used to identify uniqueness SHA256
  vBFile bfile;
  vBlob  blob;
  vHash  raw(64);
  vLen  number;

begin
  vBFile := BFilename(pOracleDir, pFilename);
  DBMS_LOB.Open(vBFile);
  vLen := DBMS_LOB.GetLength(vBFile);
  DBMS_LOB.CreateTemporary(vBlob, True, DBMS_LOB.Call);
  DBMS_LOB.LoadFromFile(vBlob, vBFile, vLen, 1, 1);
  vHash := DBMS_CRYPTO.Hash(vBlob, DBMS_CRYPTO.HASH_SH256);
  DBMS_LOB.FreeTemporary(vBlob);
  vBlob := null;
  DBMS_LOB.Close(vBFile);
  return vHash;
exception
  when OTHERS then
    if vBlob is not null then
      DBMS_LOB.FreeTemporary(vBlob);
    end if;
    if DBMS_LOB.FileIsOpen(vBFile) = 1 then
      DBMS_LOB.Close(vBFile);
    end if;
    raise;
end;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE DOCLIGHT.blob_to_file (i_dir    IN VARCHAR2,
                                          i_file   IN VARCHAR2,
                                          i_blob   IN BLOB)
AS
   l_file       UTL_FILE.file_type;
   l_buffer     RAW (32767);
   l_amount     BINARY_INTEGER := 32767;
   l_pos        INTEGER := 1;
   l_blob_len   INTEGER;
BEGIN
   l_blob_len := DBMS_LOB.getlength (i_blob);

   l_file :=
      UTL_FILE.fopen (i_dir,
                      i_file,
                      'WB'/*,
                      32767*/);

   WHILE l_pos < l_blob_len
   LOOP
      DBMS_LOB.read (i_blob,
                     l_amount,
                     l_pos,
                     l_buffer);
      UTL_FILE.put_raw (l_file, l_buffer, TRUE);
      l_pos := l_pos + l_amount;
   END LOOP;

   UTL_FILE.fclose (l_file);
EXCEPTION
   WHEN OTHERS
   THEN
      IF UTL_FILE.is_open (l_file)
      THEN
         UTL_FILE.fclose (l_file);
      END IF;

      RAISE;
END blob_to_file;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE procedure DOCLIGHT.cancella_doc (PDoc in varchar2,PCommit in varchar2 default 'S',PCancPst in varchar2 default 'S',PCancCar in varchar2 default 'S') is
    VCnt binary_integer;
    begin
    --
    --  Cancello TD010, TD013, TD003, TD001, TD000
    --
        if PCancCar = 'S' then
          select count(*)
            into VCnt
            from td010_doc_car
           where cd_doc = PDoc;
          --
          if VCnt > 0 then
            delete from td010_doc_car
             where cd_doc = PDoc;
          end if;
          --
        end if;
    --
        select count(*)
          into VCnt
          from td016_doc_all
         where cd_doc = PDoc;
        --
        if VCnt > 0 then
          delete from td016_doc_all
           where cd_doc = PDoc;
        end if;
    --
        select count(*)
          into VCnt
          from td016_doc_all
         where cd_doc_all = PDoc;
        --
        if VCnt > 0 then
          delete from td016_doc_all
           where cd_doc_all = PDoc;
        end if;
    --
        select count(*)
          into VCnt
          from td013_doc_pad
         where cd_doc = PDoc;
        --
        if VCnt > 0 then
          delete from td013_doc_pad
           where cd_doc = PDoc;
        end if;
    --
        select count(*)
          into VCnt
          from td013_doc_pad
         where cd_doc_pad = PDoc;
        --
        if VCnt > 0 then
          delete from td013_doc_pad
           where cd_doc_pad = PDoc;
        end if;
    --
        select count(*)
          into VCnt
          from td003_doc_key
         where cd_doc = PDoc;
        --
        if VCnt > 0 then
          delete from td003_doc_key
           where cd_doc = PDoc;
        end if;
    --
        if PCancPst = 'S' then
          select count(*)
            into VCnt
            from td012_doc_pst
           where cd_doc = PDoc;
          --
          if VCnt > 0 then
            delete from td012_doc_pst
             where cd_doc = PDoc;
          end if;
        end if;
    --
        select count(*)
          into VCnt
          from td001_doc_det
         where cd_doc = PDoc;
        --
        if VCnt > 0 then
          delete from td001_doc_det
           where cd_doc = PDoc;
        end if;
    --
        select count(*)
          into VCnt
          from td000_doc
         where name = PDoc;
        --
        if VCnt > 0 then
          delete from td000_doc
          where name = PDoc;
        end if;
    --
        delete from WF_DOC_APPR_REQUEST t where t.cd_doc = PDoc;
        if PCommit = 'S' then
          commit;
        end if;
    --
end cancella_doc;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE procedure DOCLIGHT.cancella_genpdf is
begin
  delete from genpdf_store_blob t where t.created_date < sysdate-2;
  commit;
end cancella_genpdf;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.can_send_ruo(pc_soc in varchar2, pc_usr in varchar2, pc_ruo in varchar2, p_id in number default null) return varchar2 is
  cnt            number;
begin
  --
  -- E' un ruolo della mia area
  --
  select count(*)
    into cnt
   from doc_web_usr_are
  where c_soc = pc_soc
    and c_are in (select c_are
                    from doc_web_usr_are
                   where  c_soc = pc_soc
                     and c_ruo = pc_ruo
                     and c_usr = pc_usr);

  if cnt>0 then return 'S'; end if;

  --
  -- E' un ruolo segreteria con flag f_abi_inv = 'N'
  --
  select count(*)
  into cnt
  from td208_ruo_are t208
  where t208.c_ruo = pc_ruo
    and t208.c_soc = pc_soc
    and nvl(t208.f_seg, 'N') = 'S'
    and nvl(t208.f_abi_inv, 'N') = 'N';

  if cnt>0 then return 'S'; end if;

  --
  -- E' un ruolo dell'area per cui è contrassegnato con f_abi_inv='S'
  select count(*)
  into cnt
  from td208_ruo_are t208
  where t208.c_soc = pc_soc
    and t208.c_are in
        (select tint.c_are
           from td208_ruo_are tint
          where tint.c_soc = pc_soc
            and tint.c_ruo = pc_ruo
            and nvl(tint.f_abi_inv, 'N') = 'S');

  if cnt>0 then return 'S'; end if;

  --
  -- E' ruolo a cui è stato inviato il documento
  if p_id is not null then
    select count(*)
    into cnt
      from td202_doc_ric
     where c_soc = pc_soc
       and c_id  = p_id
       and c_ruo = pc_ruo;
  end if;

  if cnt>0 then return 'S'; end if;

  return 'N';
end can_send_ruo;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.CHECK_DOC_MEMO(PDoc in varchar2 default null, PUsr in varchar2 default null) return varchar2 is
vRet number := 0; -- 0 Non esiste - 1 Esiste
begin
    if PDoc is not null and PUsr is not null then
        begin
            select distinct 1 into vRet 
              from td012_doc_pst where cd_doc = PDoc;
              -- AND controllo se PUsr con cui sono loggato ha i privilegi necessari per visualizzare il Memo?
        exception when others then
            vRet := 0;
        end;
    end if;
    return vRet;
end CHECK_DOC_MEMO;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE procedure DOCLIGHT.clear_db is
  cursor file_non_pres is 
       select t.* from TD000_DOC t where esiste_file(t.name)='N';
begin
  for f in file_non_pres loop
    cancella_doc(PDoc     => f.name,
                 PCommit  => 'S',
                 PCancPst => 'S',
                 PCancCar => 'S');
  end loop;
  
end clear_db;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE DOCLIGHT.CLOB_TO_FILE(
    p_fileName IN VARCHAR2,
    p_dir      IN VARCHAR2,
    p_clob     IN CLOB )
AS
  v_lob_image_id NUMBER;
  v_clob CLOB := p_clob;
  v_buffer RAW (32767);
  c_buffer VARCHAR2 (32767);
  v_buffer_size BINARY_INTEGER;
  v_amount BINARY_INTEGER;
  v_pos       NUMBER (38) := 1;
  v_clob_size INTEGER;
  v_out_file UTL_FILE.file_type;
BEGIN
  --dbms_output.put_line('Start Time: ' || TO_CHAR(sysdate,('YYYY/MM/DD hh24:Mi:ssss')));
  v_pos       := 1;
  v_clob_size := DBMS_LOB.GETLENGTH (v_clob);
  --IF (v_clob_size  < 32767) THEN
  -- v_buffer_size := v_clob_size;
  -- ELSE
  -- v_buffer_size := 32767;
  --END IF;
  v_buffer_size              := 32767;
  v_amount                   := v_buffer_size;
  IF (dbms_lob.isopen(v_clob) = 0) THEN
    dbms_lob.open(v_clob,dbms_lob.lob_readonly);
  END IF;
  v_out_file     := UTL_FILE.fopen (p_dir,p_fileName , 'WB', max_linesize => 32767);
  WHILE v_amount >= v_buffer_size
  LOOP
    DBMS_LOB.read (v_clob, v_amount, v_pos, c_buffer);
    --c_buffer := DBMS_LOB.SUBSTR(v_clob, v_amount, v_pos);
    v_buffer := UTL_RAW.CAST_TO_RAW(c_buffer);
    v_pos    := v_pos + v_amount;
    UTL_FILE.put_raw (v_out_file, v_buffer, TRUE);
    UTL_FILE.fflush (v_out_file);
  END LOOP;
  UTL_FILE.fflush (v_out_file);
  UTL_FILE.fclose (v_out_file);
  IF ( dbms_lob.isopen(v_clob) = 1 ) THEN
    dbms_lob.close(v_clob);
  END IF;
  --dbms_output.put_line('End Time: ' || TO_CHAR(sysdate,('YYYY/MM/DD hh24:Mi:ssss')));
EXCEPTION
WHEN OTHERS THEN
  IF ( dbms_lob.isopen(v_clob) = 1 ) THEN
    dbms_lob.close(v_clob);
  END IF;
  RAISE;
END;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.containsTxt(PBlob in Blob, Ptxt in varchar2) return varchar2 is
  v_pos number;
    v_file_clob clob;
    v_file_size integer := dbms_lob.lobmaxsize;
    v_dest_offset integer := 1;
    v_src_offset integer := 1;
    v_blob_csid number := dbms_lob.default_csid;
    v_lang_context number := dbms_lob.default_lang_ctx;
    v_warning integer;
    v_length number;

  begin

     dbms_lob.createtemporary(v_file_clob, true);

     dbms_lob.converttoclob(v_file_clob,
    PBlob,
    v_file_size,
    v_dest_offset,
    v_src_offset,
    v_blob_csid,
    v_lang_context,
    v_warning);

    v_pos := DBMS_LOB.INSTR(v_file_clob, Ptxt);

    if v_pos>0 then
      return 'S';
    else
      return 'N';
    end if;

end containsTxt;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE procedure DOCLIGHT.crea_pacchetti_conservazione is
    cursor pacchetti is
      select t.n_id_idc, t.c_tip_pac
        from tcs010_idc t
       where t.c_sta_idc = 'E';
  begin
    for p in pacchetti loop
      if p.c_tip_pac = 'PDV' then
         CS0010_PDV.crea_pdv(p.n_id_idc);
      elsif p.c_tip_pac = 'PDA' then
         CS0011_PDA.crea_pda(p.n_id_idc);
      elsif p.c_tip_pac = 'PDD' then
         CS0012_PDD.crea_pdd(p.n_id_idc);
      end if;
    end loop;
end crea_pacchetti_conservazione;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE procedure DOCLIGHT.CreateLanguageFilesUtf8  is
  l_file       utl_file.file_type;
  txt          varchar2(4000);

  cursor lingue is
    select *
      from doc_web_lin
     where c_lin<>'IT';

  cursor italiani is
    select * from doc_web_msg_trd t1 order by t1.c_msg;

  cursor messaggi(pCLinOri in varchar2, pCLinTrd in varchar2) is
   select t1.c_msg, t2.t_lin_trd
     from doc_web_msg_trd t1, doc_web_tra t2
    where t2.c_lin_ori = pCLinOri
      and t2.c_lin_trd = pCLinTrd
      and t2.t_lin_trd is not null
       and ltrim(rtrim(upper(t2.t_lin_ori)))=ltrim(rtrim(upper(t1.t_msg)))
      order by t1.c_msg;

begin
    l_file := utl_file.fopen_nchar('LANG_FILES_UTF8', 'IT.properties', 'w');
    -- ITALIANO
    for i in italiani loop
      txt := i.c_msg||'='||i.t_msg;
      utl_file.put_line_nchar(l_file, txt);
    end loop;
    utl_file.fclose(l_file);

    -- altre lingue
    for l in lingue loop
    l_file := utl_file.fopen_nchar('LANG_FILES_UTF8', l.c_lin||'.properties', 'w');
      for m in messaggi('IT', l.c_lin) loop
        txt := m.c_msg||'='||m.t_lin_trd;
        utl_file.put_line_nchar(l_file, txt);
      end loop;
    utl_file.fclose(l_file);
    end loop;

end CreateLanguageFilesUtf8;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION DOCLIGHT.DecodeBASE64(InBase64Char IN OUT NOCOPY CLOB) RETURN CLOB IS

    blob_loc BLOB;
    clob_trim CLOB;
    res CLOB;

    lang_context INTEGER := DBMS_LOB.DEFAULT_LANG_CTX;
    dest_offset INTEGER := 1;
    src_offset INTEGER := 1;
    read_offset INTEGER := 1;
    warning INTEGER;
    ClobLen INTEGER := DBMS_LOB.GETLENGTH(InBase64Char);

    amount INTEGER := 1440; -- must be a whole multiple of 4
    buffer RAW(1440);
    stringBuffer VARCHAR2(1440);
    -- BASE64 characters are always simple ASCII. Thus you get never any Mulit-Byte character and having the same size as 'amount' is sufficient

BEGIN

    IF InBase64Char IS NULL OR NVL(ClobLen, 0) = 0 THEN
        RETURN NULL;
    ELSIF ClobLen<= 32000 THEN
        RETURN UTL_RAW.CAST_TO_VARCHAR2(UTL_ENCODE.BASE64_DECODE(UTL_RAW.CAST_TO_RAW(InBase64Char)));
    END IF;
    -- UTL_ENCODE.BASE64_DECODE is limited to 32k, process in chunks if bigger

    -- Remove all NEW_LINE from base64 string
    ClobLen := DBMS_LOB.GETLENGTH(InBase64Char);
    DBMS_LOB.CREATETEMPORARY(clob_trim, TRUE);
    LOOP
        EXIT WHEN read_offset > ClobLen;
        stringBuffer := REPLACE(REPLACE(DBMS_LOB.SUBSTR(InBase64Char, amount, read_offset), CHR(13), NULL), CHR(10), NULL);
        DBMS_LOB.WRITEAPPEND(clob_trim, LENGTH(stringBuffer), stringBuffer);
        read_offset := read_offset + amount;
    END LOOP;

    read_offset := 1;
    ClobLen := DBMS_LOB.GETLENGTH(clob_trim);
    DBMS_LOB.CREATETEMPORARY(blob_loc, TRUE);
    LOOP
        EXIT WHEN read_offset > ClobLen;
        buffer := UTL_ENCODE.BASE64_DECODE(UTL_RAW.CAST_TO_RAW(DBMS_LOB.SUBSTR(clob_trim, amount, read_offset)));
        DBMS_LOB.WRITEAPPEND(blob_loc, DBMS_LOB.GETLENGTH(buffer), buffer);
        read_offset := read_offset + amount;
    END LOOP;

    DBMS_LOB.CREATETEMPORARY(res, TRUE);
    DBMS_LOB.CONVERTTOCLOB(res, blob_loc, DBMS_LOB.LOBMAXSIZE, dest_offset, src_offset,  DBMS_LOB.DEFAULT_CSID, lang_context, warning);

    DBMS_LOB.FREETEMPORARY(blob_loc);
    DBMS_LOB.FREETEMPORARY(clob_trim);
    RETURN res;

END DecodeBASE64;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE procedure DOCLIGHT.distribuisci_documenti_pratica(psoc in varchar2,ppra in varchar2,psot_pra in varchar2,pusr_resp in varchar2) is
 cursor cdoc is
   select c_id
     from td206_leg_prot_pra t
    where t.c_sot_pra = psot_pra
      and t.c_pra = ppra
      and t.c_soc = psoc;
 function esiste_doc_dis(pid in varchar2,psoc in varchar2,pruo in varchar2) return varchar2 is
     VCount number;
   begin
     select count(*)
       into VCount
       from td202_doc_ric s
      where s.c_soc = psoc
        and s.c_ruo = pruo
        and s.c_id = pid;
     if VCount > 0 then return('S');
     else return('N');
     end if;
   end esiste_doc_dis;
begin
  -- per ogni documento della sottopratica
  for rdoc in cdoc loop
    --se documento non e stato distribuito, lo distribuisco
    if esiste_doc_dis(rdoc.c_id,psoc,pusr_resp) = 'N' then
      insert into td202_doc_ric (c_soc,c_ruo,d_ric,c_sta, d_pri_vis,d_ult_vis, c_id)
          values (PSoc, pusr_resp,sysdate,'N',null,null,rdoc.c_Id);
    end if;
  end loop;
end distribuisci_documenti_pratica;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION DOCLIGHT.ean13 (PNumPro in varchar2) return varchar2 is
  VCodEan varchar2(13);
  VCod    varchar2(12);
  VNum    number;
begin
  VCod := PNumPro;
  
  VNum  := 3*(to_number(substr(VCod,2,1))+ to_number(substr(VCod,4,1))+ to_number(substr(VCod,6,1))+
              to_number(substr(VCod,8,1))+to_number(substr(VCod,10,1))+to_number(substr(VCod,12,1)))+
              to_number(substr(VCod,1,1))+to_number(substr(VCod,3,1))+to_number(substr(VCod,5,1))+
              to_number(substr(VCod,7,1))+to_number(substr(VCod,9,1))+to_number(substr(VCod,11,1));

  VNum  := mod(VNum,10);
  if VNum > 0 then
     VNum := 10-Vnum;
  end if;
  VCodEan := VCod||to_char(VNum);
  return VCodEan;
end ean13;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.esiste_file(pName in varchar2) return varchar2 is
  vDoc td000_doc%ROWTYPE;
begin
    select t.*
      into vDoc
      from td000_doc t
     where t.name = pName;
     
    if vDoc.Content_Type = 'BLOB' then
      if dbms_lob.getlength(vDoc.Blob_Content)>0 then 
        return 'Y';
      end if;
    else
      if dbms_lob.fileexists(vDoc.Bfile_Content)=1 then
        return 'Y';
      end if;
    end if;  
    
    return 'N';                 
  exception when others then
    return 'N';
end esiste_file;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.esiste_immagine(p_file in varchar2) return varchar2 is
   VEsiste varchar2(1);
   begin
     select 'S'
       into VEsiste
       from td000_doc
      where name = p_file;
     return(VEsiste);
     exception when others then return('N');
   end esiste_immagine;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.esiste_protocollo(PN_Prot         in varchar2,
                                             PN_Ann_prot     in number,
                                             PC_Prot         in varchar2,
                                             PC_Tip_Prot     in varchar2,
                                             PC_Soc          in varchar2
                           ) return varchar2 is

      cnt number;
   begin

    select count(*)
      into cnt
      from td033_prot
     where c_prot = PC_Prot
       and n_ann_prot = PN_Ann_prot
       and n_prot = PN_Prot
       and c_soc = PC_Soc
       and c_tip_prot = PC_Tip_Prot;

    if cnt>0 then return 'S';
    else return 'N';
    end if;

end esiste_protocollo;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.extractFattPassOri(pcd_doc in varchar2)return clob is
  vEnc XMLType;
  l_output_blob cLOB;

  BDoc          Blob;

begin
  select decode(t.content_type, 'BFILE', crypto.decr_tipo(pkdoc_new.get_tip_doc(t.name),utl_bfile.bFileToBLob(t.bfile_content)), t.blob_content)
    into BDoc
  from td000_doc t
  where name = pcd_doc;

  if crypto.isEnc(BDoc)='S' then
    select
     XMLQuery('/FatturaElettronicaPassiva/FatturaOriginale/FatturaXml/text()'
             PASSING t.msg
           RETURNING CONTENT)
           into vEnc
        from
        (select XMLType(crypto.decr(BDoc),
                 1 /* this is your character set ID.
                           1 == USASCII */
               ) as msg
         from td000_doc t where name =pcd_doc)
        t;
  else
    select
     XMLQuery('/FatturaElettronicaPassiva/FatturaOriginale/FatturaXml/text()'
             PASSING t.msg
           RETURNING CONTENT)
           into vEnc
        from
        (select XMLType(BDoc,
                 1 /* this is your character set ID.
                           1 == USASCII */
               ) as msg
         from td000_doc t where name =pcd_doc)
        t;
  end if;



    l_output_blob := vEnc.getClobVal();


    return DecodeBASE64(l_output_blob);

end extractFattPassOri;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.ExtractXmlFromP7m(PDocIn in blob) return blob is
    gFConvName    varchar2(100);
    gConvDir      varchar2(32)  := 'CONVDIR';
    vBF           bFile;
    gConvDirPath  varchar2(100);
    gP7mCmd       varchar2(100) := 'p7m2xml'||doc_web_utl.getExtFile('.cmd');  -- Script per la conversione il file dev essere in gConvDir
    gOS           varchar2(1)   := doc_web_utl.getOS;

    vRes          number;
begin
      begin
        select t.directory_path
          into gConvDirPath
          from all_directories t
         where t.directory_name = gConvDir;
      end;

      if gOS = 'W' then
        gFConvName := to_char(sysdate,'yyyymmddhh24miss');
        utl_bfile.bLobToBFile(PDocIn, gConvDir, gFConvName||'.xml.p7m', vBF);
        vRes := fexeccmd(gConvDirPath||gP7mCmd||' '||gFConvName);
      else
        gFConvName := 'file';
        utl_bfile.bLobToBFile(PDocIn, gConvDir, gFConvName||'.xml.p7m', vBF);
        vRes := fexeccmd(gConvDirPath||gP7mCmd);
      end if;
      --
      if vRes=0 then
         vBF  := bfilename(gConvDir, gFConvName||'.xml');
         return loadblobfrombfile(vBF);
      else
        return null;
      end if;

end ExtractXmlFromP7m;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE procedure DOCLIGHT.file_compose(PDocName out varchar2, PCIds in varchar2, PBcode in varchar2 default null) is
   type VArray IS table of VARCHAR2(100) index by BINARY_INTEGER;

    Len binary_integer;
    Tab VArray;
    VTmpDoc  TD000_TMP_DOC%Rowtype;
    Usr      varchar2(200);

 procedure ListToTable (PList in varchar2, PSep in varchar2, PLen out binary_integer, PTab out VArray)
  is
   VInd  binary_integer;
   VTab  VArray;
   VFin  binary_integer;
   VList varchar2(32000);
   VSep  varchar2(1);
  begin
    VTab.delete;
    VInd := 0;
    if PList is null or length(nvl(PSep,',')) > 1 then
      PTab := VTab;
      PLen := VInd;
      return;
    end if;  
    VSep  := nvl(PSep,',');
    VList := PList;
    if substr(VList,1,1) <> VSep then
      VList := VSep||Vlist;
    end if;  
    if substr(VList,length(VList),1) <> VSep then
      VList := Vlist||VSep;
    end if;  
    loop
      VFin := instr(VList,VSep,1,2);
      exit when VFin = 0;
      VInd := VInd+1;
      VTab(Vind) := substr(VList,2,VFin-2);
      VList := substr(Vlist,Vfin);
    end loop;
    PTab := VTab;
    PLen := VInd;
  end ListToTable;
    
  procedure drawImage(image in blob, imageW in number, imageH in number, areaW in number, areaH in number, x in number, y in number) is
    nRatioW   number;
    nRatioH   number;
    nRatio    number;
    w         number;
    h         number;
    xcenter   number;
  begin
        nRatioW := imageW/areaW;
        if areaH = 0 then
           nRatioH := 0;
        else
           nRatioH := imageH/areaH;
        end if;
        if nRatioW >= nRatioH then
          nRatio := nRatioW;
        else
          nRatio := nRatioH;
        end if;

       w := imageW;
       h := imageH;

       if nRatio>1 then
         w := imageW/nRatio;
         h := imageH/nRatio;
       end if;

       xcenter := x + areaW/2-w/2;

       genpdf.DrawImage(image, xcenter+1, y+1, w, h);

  end drawImage;

  
      
begin
  begin
      genpdf.init('A4', 'P');
      genpdf.setmargin(1,1,1,1);
      genpdf.SetFillColor(215,215,215);
      genpdf.SetFont('Arial',null,8);

      ListToTable(PCIds,';',Len,Tab);
      
      for l in 1..Len loop 
       select * 
         into VTmpDoc
         from td000_tmp_doc
        where c_id = Tab(l);

        Usr:=VTmpDoc.c_Usr_Id;
        genpdf.NewPage;
        drawImage(VTmpDoc.t_Blob, 208, 295, 208, 295, 0, 0);
      end loop;
      
      genpdf.CreateDocument('T',   PDocName);
      
      for l in 1..Len loop 
       delete from td000_tmp_doc
        where c_id = Tab(l);
      end loop;
      
      insert into td000_tmp_doc (c_id, t_blob, c_usr_id, doc_size, f_cmp, t_ext, f_Zebra_Prot, d_load)
      (select Tab(1), blob_file, Usr, 1, 'S', 'pdf', VTmpDoc.f_Zebra_Prot, sysdate from genpdf_store_blob where cdoc=PDocName);
      
      if PBcode is not null then
        update td000_tmp_doc set c_id=PBcode where c_id=Tab(1);
      end if;
      
      commit;
      
   exception when others then
     dbms_output.put_line(sqlerrM);
     PDocName:=null;
   end;      
end file_compose;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION DOCLIGHT.file_to_blob (i_dir IN VARCHAR2, i_filename IN VARCHAR2)
   RETURN BLOB
AS
   l_bfile   BFILE;
   l_blob    BLOB;
BEGIN
   DBMS_LOB.createtemporary (l_blob, FALSE);
   l_bfile := BFILENAME (i_dir, i_filename);
   DBMS_LOB.fileopen (l_bfile, DBMS_LOB.file_readonly);
   DBMS_LOB.loadfromfile (l_blob, l_bfile, DBMS_LOB.getlength (l_bfile));
   DBMS_LOB.fileclose (l_bfile);

   RETURN l_blob;
EXCEPTION
   WHEN OTHERS
   THEN
      IF DBMS_LOB.fileisopen (l_bfile) = 1
      THEN
         DBMS_LOB.fileclose (l_bfile);
      END IF;

      DBMS_LOB.freetemporary (l_blob);
        RETURN EMPTY_BLOB();
END file_to_blob;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.gdof0001(usr in varchar2,doc in varchar2,ope in varchar2) return number is
  VCount number;
begin
  select count(distinct cd_doc)
    into VCount
    from td013_doc_pad
   where cd_doc_pad = doc
     and gdok0001.check_abi_doc(usr,cd_doc,ope) = 'S';
  return(VCount);
end gdof0001;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.gdof0003(usr in varchar2,doc in varchar2,ope in varchar2) return number is
  VCount number;
begin
  select count(distinct cd_doc_pad)
    into VCount
    from td013_doc_pad
   where cd_doc = doc
     and cd_doc_pad is not null
     and gdok0001.check_abi_doc(usr,cd_doc_pad,ope) = 'S';
  return(VCount);
end gdof0003;
;
