CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.get_barcode_prot(Psoc in varchar2,PAnn in number,PNum in number,PCProt in varchar2) return varchar2 is
    VRet varchar2(10);
  begin
    begin
      select lpad(t.n_code_prot,2,'0')||substr(PAnn,3)||lpad(PNum,6,'0')
        into VRet
        from td042_tip_prot t
       where t.c_tip_prot = PCProt
         and t.n_ann_prot = PAnn
         and t.c_soc = Psoc;
      exception when others then VRet := null;
    end;
    return(VRet);
  end get_barcode_prot;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.getbfilename(PBFile in bfile, PTip in varchar2 default null) return varchar2 is
    VDir   varchar2(50);
    VFName varchar2(2000);
  begin
    --
    dbms_lob.filegetname(PBFile, VDir, VFName);
    --
    if PTip is null then
      return VDir||'§'||VFName;
    elsif PTip = 'F' then
      return VFName;
    elsif PTip = 'D' then
      return VDir;
    else
      return null;
    end if;
  exception
    when others then
      return null;
  end;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.get_compose_tree_tag(pc_soc in varchar2, pc_tip in varchar2, pc_node in varchar2) return VARCHAR2 is

  vret varchar2(1000) := '';

  cursor nodi is
    select t.* from
    (select ti.*--, level, decode(t_nod_pad, null, t_nod, t_nod_pad||'.'||t_nod)
      from tcs027_tag_xsd ti
     where c_tip = pc_tip
       and c_soc=pc_soc) t
   connect by prior t.t_nod_pad=t.t_nod
     start with t.t_nod=pc_node
     order siblings by t_nod;

begin
  for n in nodi loop
    vret := n.t_nod||'.'||vRet;
  end loop;

  if length(vret)>1 then
    vret := substr(vret, 1, length(vret)-1);
  end if;

  return(vret);
end;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.getConsApprDirByCas(pCIdCas in varchar2) return varchar2 is
  vRet varchar2(200) := 'ARCHIDOC_APPR';
  vSoc tcs010_idc.c_soc%TYPE;
begin
  /* il nome è quello relativo alle pec per mantenere similitudine nei package TCS002,
  ma in realtà non si va per casella ma per società tramite nIdIdc */
  -- root base della conservazione
   select t.c_soc
    into vSoc
    from tcs010_idc t
   where t.n_id_idc = pCIdCas;

  if vSoc='STF' then
    vRet := 'ARCHIDOC_APPR_STF';
  elsif vSoc='OKG' then
    vRet := 'ARCHIDOC_APPR_OKG';
  elsif vSoc='TCF' then
    vRet := 'ARCHIDOC_APPR_TCF';
  end if;

  return(vRet);
end getConsApprDirByCas;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.getConsDirByCas(pCIdCas in varchar2) return varchar2 is
  vRet varchar2(200);
  vSoc tcs010_idc.c_soc%TYPE;
begin
  /* il nome è quello relativo alle pec per mantenere similitudine nei package TCS002,
  ma in realtà non si va per casella ma per società tramite nIdIdc */
  -- root base della conservazione
  select t.c_arc_root_dir
  into vRet
  from TCS000_APPL t
  where nvl(t.d_fin, sysdate)>=sysdate;

  select t.c_soc
    into vSoc
    from tcs010_idc t
   where t.n_id_idc = pCIdCas;

  if vSoc='STF' then
    vRet := 'ARCHIDOC_STF';
  elsif vSoc='OKG' then
    vRet := 'ARCHIDOC_OKG';
  elsif vSoc='TCF' then
    vRet := 'ARCHIDOC_TCF';
  end if;

  return(vRet);
end getConsDirByCas;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.getConsDirByUsr(pCUsr in varchar2) return varchar2 is
  vRet varchar2(200);
begin

  -- root base della conservazione
  select t.c_arc_root_dir
  into vRet
  from TCS000_APPL t;

  return(vRet);
end getConsDirByUsr;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.getConsPathByCas(pCIdCas in varchar2) return varchar2 is
  vRet varchar2(200);
  vCArcRootDirSoc varchar2(200);
begin
  vCArcRootDirSoc := getConsDirByCas(pCIdCas);
  begin
    select ad.DIRECTORY_PATH
       into vRet
       from all_directories ad
       where ad.DIRECTORY_NAME = vCArcRootDirSoc;

    if instr(vRet, '\', -1)=length(vRet) then
      vRet := substr(vRet, 1, length(vRet)-1);
    end if;

  exception when others then
    vRet := 'F:\ARCHIDOC';
  end;
  return(vRet);
end getConsPathByCas;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.getConsPathByUsr(pCUsr in varchar2) return varchar2 is
  vRet varchar2(200);
  vCArcRootDirSoc varchar2(1000);
begin
  vCArcRootDirSoc := getConsDirByUsr(pCUsr);
  begin
    select ad.DIRECTORY_PATH
       into vRet
       from all_directories ad
       where ad.DIRECTORY_NAME = vCArcRootDirSoc;
  exception when others then
    null;
  end;
  return(vRet);
end getConsPathByUsr;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.getConsPathTomcatByCas(pCIdCas in varchar2) return varchar2 is
  vRet varchar2(200);
  vSoc tcs010_idc.c_soc%TYPE;

begin

  -- root base della conservazione
  select t.c_arc_root_path
  into vRet
  from TCS000_APPL t
  where nvl(t.d_fin, sysdate)>=sysdate;

  if instr(vRet, '\', -1)=length(vRet) then
      vRet := substr(vRet, 1, length(vRet)-1);
  end if;

  select t.c_soc
    into vSoc
    from tcs010_idc t
   where t.n_id_idc = pCIdCas;

  if vSoc='STF' then
    vRet := vRet||'\STF';
  elsif vSoc='OKG' then
    vRet := vRet||'\OKG';
  elsif vSoc='TCF' then
    vRet := vRet||'\TCF';
  end if;

  return(vRet);
end;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.getConsPathTomcatByUsr(pCUsr in varchar2) return varchar2 is
  vRet varchar2(200);
begin

  -- root base della conservazione
  select t.c_arc_root_path
  into vRet
  from TCS000_APPL t;

  return(vRet);
end getConsPathTomcatByUsr;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.getDocExtension(pname in varchar2) return varchar2 is
  vRet varchar2(500);
  punto          number;
  vExt           varchar2(100);
  cnt            number;
begin
  punto := instr(pname, '.', -1); -- last punto
  if punto = 0 then -- non ha punti
    begin
      select '.'||max(mt.estensione)
        into vRet
        from td000_doc t0, mime_types mt
       where upper(mt.mime_application )=upper(t0.mime_type)
        and t0.name = pname;
       
       return vRet;
     exception when others then -- mime application non trovata
       return '';
     end;
  end if;
  
  vExt := substr(pname, punto); -- estensione
  select count(*) 
    into cnt
    from mime_types mt
    where upper(vExt) = upper(mt.estensione);
    
  if cnt>0 then -- estensione valida
    return '.'||vExt;
  end if;
  
   -- estensione non valida
   begin
      select '.'||max(mt.estensione)
        into vRet
        from td000_doc t0, mime_types mt
       where upper(mt.mime_application )=upper(t0.mime_type)
        and t0.name = pname;
       
       return vRet;
   exception when others then -- mime application non trovata
     return '';
   end;
     
   return '';
  
end getDocExtension;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION DOCLIGHT.get_file_name (bf BFILE) RETURN VARCHAR2 is
    dir_alias VARCHAR2(255);
    file_name VARCHAR2(255);
    BEGIN
      IF bf is NULL THEN
        RETURN NULL;
      ELSE
        DBMS_LOB.FILEGETNAME (bf, dir_alias, file_name);
        RETURN file_name;
      END IF;
  END;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.get_IdRow_Cons (PC_TIP in VARCHAR2, PC_Soc in VARCHAR2, PKey1 in varchar2 default null
       , PKey2 in varchar2 default null, PKey3 in varchar2 default null, PKey4 in varchar2 default null, PKey5 in varchar2 default null) return varchar2 is
  vRet varchar2(4000);
  vSep varchar(1) := '_';
begin
  if pc_tip='ORD' then
    -- pKey1 cliente
    -- pKey2 anno ordine
    -- pKey3 numero ordine
    vRet := pc_soc||vSep||pKey1||vSep||PKey2||vSep||PKey3;
  end if;
  return(vRet);
end ;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.get_lista_doc_sign(pNIdRic in number) return clob is
  ret clob;
  cursor documenti is
      select t.cd_doc pfname
      from Td060_Doc_Fir_sit t
     where t.c_id = pNIdRic;
begin

  for d in documenti loop
    ret := ret || d.pfname || ';';
  end loop;
  return(ret);
end;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION DOCLIGHT.get_msg(Vc_msg in number,
                 VCd_lin_trd in varchar2,
                 PTrad in varchar2 default 'N',
                 Ppar1 in varchar2 default null,
                 Ppar2 in varchar2 default null,
                 Ppar3 in varchar2 default null,
                 Ppar4 in varchar2 default null)  RETURN varchar2 IS
 Vds_lin_ori varchar2(2000);
 VText varchar2(2000);
 Vlin_ini varchar2(2000);
BEGIN
  begin
    select nvl(c_lin_ini, 'IT')
      into Vlin_ini
      from doc_web_cfg;
  	exception when no_data_found then Vlin_ini := 'IT';
  end;
 	begin
  	select t_msg
    	into Vds_lin_ori
    	from doc_web_msg_trd
  	 where c_msg = Vc_msg;
  	exception when no_data_found then Vds_lin_ori := null;
  end;
  VText := traduci(Vlin_ini,Vds_lin_ori,Vcd_lin_trd);
  if PTrad = 'N' then  -- non va tradotto
  	VText := replace(replace(replace(replace(VText,'§1§',nvl(Ppar1,' ')),'§2§',nvl(Ppar2,' ')),'§3§',nvl(Ppar3,' ')),'§4§',nvl(Ppar4,' '));
  else
  	VText := replace(replace(replace(replace(VText,'§1§',traduci(Vlin_ini,Ppar1,Vcd_lin_trd)),'§2§',traduci(Vlin_ini,Ppar2,Vcd_lin_trd)),'§3§',traduci(Vlin_ini,Ppar3,Vcd_lin_trd)),'§4§',traduci(Vlin_ini,Ppar4,Vcd_lin_trd));
  end if;
  return(VText);
END;
;

end getPecBFileDirByCas;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.hextonum (PH in varchar2) return number is
    VRet number := 0;
  begin
     for i in reverse 1..length(PH) loop
       case substr(upper(PH),i,1)
       when 'F' then VRet:=VRet+15*power(16,length(PH)-i);
       when 'E' then VRet:=VRet+14*power(16,length(PH)-i);
       when 'D' then VRet:=VRet+13*power(16,length(PH)-i);
       when 'C' then VRet:=VRet+12*power(16,length(PH)-i);
       when 'B' then VRet:=VRet+11*power(16,length(PH)-i);
       when 'A' then VRet:=VRet+10*power(16,length(PH)-i);
       else VRet:=VRet+to_number(substr(upper(PH),i,1))*power(16,length(PH)-i);
       end case;
     end loop;
     return VRet;
  end hextonum;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.isDocSignable(pName in varchar2) return varchar2 is
  nIdPdv  number;
  vRet    varchar2(1);
  nCnt    number;
begin
    select t.n_id_pdv
      into nIdPdv
      from td000_doc t
     where t.name=pName;

  if nIdPdv is not null then
    return 'N';
  end if;

  select count(*)
    into nCnt
    from td060_doc_fir_sit t
    where t.cd_doc = pName;

  if nCnt > 0 then
    return 'N';
  end if;

  vRet := isdocsigned(pName);
  if vRet = 'S' then
    return 'N';
  end if;

  return('S');
end isDocSignable;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.isDocSigned(pName in varchar2) return varchar2 is
  FunctionResult varchar2(1);
  BDoc           blob;
  vMime           varchar2(100);
begin
  begin
    select CRYPTO.DECR(decode(t.content_type, 'BFILE', loadBlobFromBFile(t.bfile_content), t.blob_content)), t.mime_type
      into BDoc, vMime
      from td000_doc t
     where t.name=pName;

    if lower(vMime) in ('application/x-pkcs7-mime', 'application/pkcs7-signature') then
      return 'S';
    end if;

    return containstxt(BDoc, 'Signature');
  exception when others then
    return 'N';
  end;

end isDocSigned;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.isDocStampable(pName in varchar2) return varchar2 is
  FunctionResult varchar2(1);
  BDoc           blob;
  vMime           varchar2(100);
begin
  begin
    select crypto.decr(t.blob_content), t.mime_type
      into BDoc, vMime
      from td000_doc t
     where t.name=pName;
     
    if upper(vMime) not in ('APPLICATION/PDF','TEXT/HTML') then
      return 'N';
    end if; 
    
    if dbms_lob.instr(BDoc, utl_raw.cast_to_raw('/ETSI.CAdES.detached'))>0 then
      return 'N';
    end if;

  exception when others then
    return 'N';
  end;
  
  return 'S';

end isDocStampable;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.isEan13(PBCode in varchar2) return varchar2 is
  VBCodeNum        number;
  VCheck           varchar2(13);
  vBCode           varchar2(100);
  dot              number;
begin
  if PBCode is null then
    return 'N';
  end if;

  
  vBCode := PBCode;
  dot := instr(vBCode, '.', -1)-1;
  if dot>0 then
    vBCode := substr(PBCode, 1, dot);
  end if;

  if length(vBCode)!=13 then
    return 'N';
  end if;

  begin
    select to_number(vBCode)
      into VBCodeNum
      from dual;
  exception when others then
    return 'N';
  end;

  select ean13(substr(vBCode, 1, 12))
    into VCheck
    from dual;

  if vBCode=VCheck then
    return 'S';
  else
    return 'N';
  end if;

end;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.isSocInGruppo(pCSoc in varchar2 default null, pCGrp in varchar2 default null) return varchar2 is
  cnt  number;
begin
  select count(*)
    into cnt 
  from td058_grp_soc t
  where t.c_grp = nvl(pCGrp,v('PCGRP'))
    and t.c_soc = nvl(pCSoc, v('PCSOC'));
  
  if cnt>0 then
    return 'S';
  else
    return 'N';
  end if;
end isSocInGruppo;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE DOCLIGHT.leggi_cookie(nome in varchar2,valore out varchar2) IS
   v_cookie owa_cookie.cookie;
BEGIN
    v_cookie := owa_cookie.get(nome);
    --owa_util.mime_header('text/html', FALSE);
    --owa_util.http_header_close;
    if v_cookie.num_vals > 0 then
       valore := v_cookie.vals(1);
    else
       valore := null;
    end if;
END;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION DOCLIGHT.loadBlobFromBFile(inBFile in BFILE) RETURN BLOB AS
  dest_loc  BLOB := empty_blob();
  src_loc   BFILE := inBFile;
BEGIN
  -- Open source binary file from OS
  DBMS_LOB.OPEN(src_loc, DBMS_LOB.LOB_READONLY);

  -- Create temporary LOB object
  DBMS_LOB.CREATETEMPORARY(
        lob_loc => dest_loc
      , cache   => true
      , dur     => dbms_lob.session
  );

  -- Open temporary lob
  DBMS_LOB.OPEN(dest_loc, DBMS_LOB.LOB_READWRITE);

  -- Load binary file into temporary LOB
  DBMS_LOB.LOADFROMFILE(
        dest_lob => dest_loc
      , src_lob  => src_loc
      , amount   => DBMS_LOB.getLength(src_loc));

  -- Close lob objects
  DBMS_LOB.CLOSE(dest_loc);
  DBMS_LOB.CLOSE(src_loc);

  -- Return temporary LOB object
  RETURN dest_loc;
END loadBlobFromBFile;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE DOCLIGHT.load_xmltype_from_url (
  p_url     IN            VARCHAR2,
  p_xmltype IN OUT NOCOPY XMLTYPE)
AS
  l_http_request   UTL_HTTP.req;
  l_http_response  UTL_HTTP.resp;
  l_clob           CLOB;
  l_text           VARCHAR2(32767);
  l_buffer         PLS_INTEGER := 10000;
BEGIN
  -- Initialize the CLOB.
  DBMS_LOB.createtemporary(l_clob, FALSE);

  -- Make a HTTP request and get the response.
  l_http_request  := UTL_HTTP.begin_request(p_url);
  l_http_response := UTL_HTTP.get_response(l_http_request);

  -- Copy the response into the CLOB.
  BEGIN
    LOOP
      UTL_HTTP.read_text(l_http_response, l_text, l_buffer);
      DBMS_LOB.writeappend (l_clob, LENGTH(l_text), l_text);
    END LOOP;
  EXCEPTION
    WHEN UTL_HTTP.end_of_body THEN
      UTL_HTTP.end_response(l_http_response);
  END;

  -- Insert the data into the table.
  p_xmltype := XMLTYPE(l_clob);

  -- Relase the resources associated with the temporary LOB.
  DBMS_LOB.freetemporary(l_clob);
EXCEPTION
  WHEN OTHERS THEN
    p_xmltype := NULL;
    UTL_HTTP.end_response(l_http_response);
    DBMS_LOB.freetemporary(l_clob);
    RAISE;
END load_xmltype_from_url;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE procedure DOCLIGHT.manual_compose(PCIds in varchar2, pSep in varchar2) is
    VTmpDoc  TD000_TMP_DOC%Rowtype;
    Usr      varchar2(200);
    NewDocName varchar2(400);
    vGenpfdInitDone varchar2(1) := 'N';
    PDocName  varchar2(400);
    vErr varchar2(4000);
    
    cursor documenti is
      select t.c_id, t.t_blob, t.c_usr_id, t.doc_size, t.t_ext, t.d_load, t.t_mime
        from td000_tmp_doc t, table(apex_string.split(PCIds, pSep)) sel
       where sel.column_value = t.c_id
       order by n_ord_cmp;

  procedure drawImage(image in blob, imageW in number, imageH in number, areaW in number, areaH in number, x in number, y in number) is
    nRatioW   number;
    nRatioH   number;
    nRatio    number;
    w         number;
    h         number;
    xcenter   number;
  begin
        nRatioW := imageW/areaW;
        if areaH = 0 then
           nRatioH := 0;
        else
           nRatioH := imageH/areaH;
        end if;
        if nRatioW >= nRatioH then
          nRatio := nRatioW;
        else
          nRatio := nRatioH;
        end if;

       w := imageW;
       h := imageH;

       if nRatio>1 then
         w := imageW/nRatio;
         h := imageH/nRatio;
       end if;

       xcenter := x + areaW/2-w/2;

       genpdf.DrawImage(image, xcenter+1, y+1, w, h);

  end drawImage;
  
begin
  begin
      apex_debug.message('PCIds='||PCIds);
      for d in documenti loop 
        if vGenpfdInitDone='N' then  -- è il primo documento
          NewDocName := d.c_id||'.pdf';
          Usr := d.c_Usr_Id;
          genpdf.init('A4', 'P');
          vGenpfdInitDone:='S';
          genpdf.setmargin(1,1,1,1);
          genpdf.SetFillColor(215,215,215);
          genpdf.SetFont('Arial',null,8);
        end if;

        genpdf.NewPage;
        select * 
          into VTmpDoc
          from td000_tmp_doc
         where c_id = d.c_id;        
        drawImage(VTmpDoc.t_Blob, 208, 295, 208, 295, 0, 0);
        apex_debug.message('Inserito '||d.c_id||', dim='||dbms_lob.getlength(VTmpDoc.t_blob));

        delete from td000_tmp_doc where c_id = d.c_id;

      end loop;

      genpdf.CreateDocument('T',   PDocName);
              
      insert into td000_tmp_doc (c_id, t_blob, c_usr_id, doc_size, f_cmp, t_ext, d_load, t_mime)
      (select NewDocName, blob_file, Usr, dbms_lob.getlength(blob_file), 'S', 'pdf', sysdate, 'application/pdf' from genpdf_store_blob where cdoc=PDocName);
      
      commit;
   exception when others then
      vErr := SUBSTR(SQLERRM, 1, 200);
     dbms_output.put_line(sqlerrM);
   end;      
end manual_compose;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.norm_cdata (PTxt in varchar2) return varchar2 is
    VStr varchar2(4000);
  begin
    VStr := null;
    if pTxt is null then
      return null;
    end if;

    for i in 1..length(PTxt) loop
      if substr(PTxt,i,1) in ('&') then
        VStr := VStr||'e';
      elsif substr(PTxt,i,1) in(chr(128),chr(141),chr(146),chr(147),chr(149),chr(160),chr(168),chr(172),chr(176),chr(177),chr(178),chr(180),chr(189),chr(191)) then
        VStr := VStr||' ';
      elsif substr(PTxt,i,1) in(chr(133),chr(192),chr(193),chr(194),chr(195),chr(196),chr(197),chr(198)) then
        VStr := VStr||'A';
      elsif substr(PTxt,i,1) in(chr(199)) then
        VStr := VStr||'C';
      elsif substr(PTxt,i,1) in(chr(200),chr(201),chr(202),chr(203)) then
        VStr := VStr||'E';
      elsif substr(PTxt,i,1) in(chr(204),chr(205),chr(206),chr(207)) then
        VStr := VStr||'I';
      elsif substr(PTxt,i,1) in(chr(208)) then
        VStr := VStr||'D';
      elsif substr(PTxt,i,1) in(chr(209)) then
        VStr := VStr||'N';
      elsif substr(PTxt,i,1) in(chr(215)) then
        VStr := VStr||'X';
      elsif substr(PTxt,i,1) in(chr(210),chr(211),chr(212),chr(213),chr(214)) then
        VStr := VStr||'O';
      elsif substr(PTxt,i,1) in(chr(216)) then
        VStr := VStr||' ';
      elsif substr(PTxt,i,1) in(chr(217),chr(218),chr(219),chr(220)) then
        VStr := VStr||'U';
      elsif substr(PTxt,i,1) in(chr(221)) then
        VStr := VStr||'Y';
      elsif substr(PTxt,i,1) in(chr(224),chr(225),chr(226),chr(227),chr(228),chr(229),chr(230)) then
        VStr := VStr||'a';
      elsif substr(PTxt,i,1) in(chr(231)) then
        VStr := VStr||'c';
      elsif substr(PTxt,i,1) in(chr(232),chr(233),chr(234),chr(235)) then
        VStr := VStr||'e';
      elsif substr(PTxt,i,1) in(chr(236),chr(237),chr(238),chr(239)) then
        VStr := VStr||'i';
      elsif substr(PTxt,i,1) in(chr(240),chr(242),chr(243),chr(244),chr(245),chr(246),chr(248)) then
        VStr := VStr||'o';
      elsif substr(PTxt,i,1) in(chr(241)) then
        VStr := VStr||'n';
      elsif substr(PTxt,i,1) in(chr(249),chr(250),chr(251),chr(252)) then
        VStr := VStr||'u';
      elsif substr(PTxt,i,1) in(chr(253),chr(255)) then
        VStr := VStr||'y';
      elsif substr(PTxt,i,1) in(chr(14844060),chr(14844061)) then
        VStr := VStr||'"';
      else
        VStr := VStr||substr(PTxt,i,1);
      end if;
    end loop;
    VStr := REPLACE(VStr, '', ' ');
    return VStr;
  end;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.NORM_FILE_NAME(PTxt in varchar2) return varchar2 is
    VRet varchar2(32000) ;
    begin
      VRet := PTxt;
      VRet := replace(VRet,'à','a');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'è','e');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'é','e');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'ì','i');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'ò','o');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'ù','u');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'À','A');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'È','E');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'Ì','I');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'Ò','O');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'Ù','U');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'Á','A');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'É','E');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'Í','I');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'Ó','O');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'Ú','U');

      VRet := replace(VRet,'Â','A');
      VRet := replace(Vret,'Ã','A');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'§',' ');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'ª',' ');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'Å','A');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'Ä','A');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'Æ','AE');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'Ç','C');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'Ê','E');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'Ë','E');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'Î','I');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'Ï','I');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'Ñ','N');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'Ô','O');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'Õ','O');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'Ö','O');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'Û','U');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'Ü','U');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'Ø','O');

      VRet := replace(VRet,'>',' ');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'<',' ');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'¿',' ');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'¿','-');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'#',' ');
      VRet := replace(VRet,':',' ');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'°',' ');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'''',' ');
      VRet := replace(VRet,';',' ');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'\',' ');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'/',' ');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'+',' ');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'"',' ');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'¿',' ');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'¿',' ');
      VRet := replace(VRet,'&',' ');


      return VRet;
end NORM_FILE_NAME;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.numtohex(p in number) return varchar2 is
    VSn integer;
    VDx integer;
    VRet varchar2(2);
  begin
    VSn := trunc(p/16);
    VDx := p-VSn*16;
    if VSn = 15 then
     VRet := 'F';
    elsif VSn = 14 then
     VRet := 'E';
    elsif VSn = 13 then
     VRet := 'D';
    elsif VSn = 12 then
     VRet := 'C';
    elsif VSn = 11 then
     VRet := 'B';
    elsif VSn = 10 then
     VRet := 'A';
    else
     VRet := to_char(VSn);
    end if;
    if VDx = 15 then
     VRet := VRet||'F';
    elsif VDx = 14 then
     VRet := VRet||'E';
    elsif VDx = 13 then
     VRet := VRet||'D';
    elsif VDx = 12 then
     VRet := VRet||'C';
    elsif VDx = 11 then
     VRet := VRet||'B';
    elsif VDx = 10 then
     VRet := VRet||'A';
    else
     VRet := VRet||to_char(VDx);
    end if;
    return VRet;
  end;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE procedure DOCLIGHT.popala_contenuti_nuove_pagine(pAppId in number) is
  cursor nuove is -- pagine inserite nel menu che non sono definite nei contenuti
    select apex_tema_abi.getPagFromUrl(pEntryTarget => le.entry_target) pag_id, le.* 
      from APEX_APPLICATION_LIST_ENTRIES le
      where application_id = pAppId
       and list_name='Desktop Navigation Menu'
       and le.entry_target is not null
       and not exists (select '*' from DOC_WEB_CON_APEX dwc
                       where dwc.c_con = le.list_entry_id
                       and dwc.application_id = le.application_id);
                       
  cursor presenti is -- pagine inserite nel menu che non sono definite nei contenuti
    select apex_tema_abi.getPagFromUrl(pEntryTarget => le.entry_target) pag_id, le.* 
      from APEX_APPLICATION_LIST_ENTRIES le
      where application_id = pAppId
       and list_name='Desktop Navigation Menu'
       and le.entry_target is not null
       and exists (select '*' from DOC_WEB_CON_APEX dwc
                       where dwc.c_con = le.list_entry_id
                       and dwc.application_id = le.application_id);                       

begin
  if pAppId is null then
    raise_application_error(-20100, 'Indicare id applicazione');
  end if;
  
  for n in nuove loop
    begin
      insert into doc_web_con (C_CON,
                                    T_CON,
                                    C_TIP,
                                    N_PAG_ID_APEX)
      values (to_char(n.list_entry_id), n.entry_text, 'A', n.pag_id);
    exception when others then 
      null;
    end;
  end loop;
  
  for p in presenti loop
    update doc_web_con dwc set dwc.t_con = p.entry_text where dwc.c_con = to_char(p.list_entry_id);
  end loop;


end popala_contenuti_nuove_pagine;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.remove_non_printable_char(pTxt in varchar2) return varchar2 is
begin
  
  return regexp_replace(pTxt, '[^[:print:]]', ' ');
end remove_non_printable_char;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.returnIDRuolo(pTxtRuolo in varchar2 default null) return number is
  vIdRuolo number;
  vEsi     number;
begin
  if pTxtRuolo is NOT NULL then
    select count(*) into vEsi from Z002_RUOLI where UPPER(T_RUOLO) = UPPER(pTxtRuolo);
    if vEsi = 0 then
      insert into Z002_RUOLI(T_RUOLO) values (UPPER(pTxtRuolo)) returning C_ID into vIdRuolo;
    else
      select C_ID into vIdRuolo from Z002_RUOLI where UPPER(T_RUOLO) = UPPER(pTxtRuolo);
    end if;
  end if;
  
  return vIdRuolo;
end returnIDRuolo;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE procedure DOCLIGHT.riempi_campi(doc in varchar2 default null) is
--
 cursor cdoc is
   select cd_doc,count(*)
     from td003_doc_key
    where (cd_doc = doc or doc is null)
    group by cd_doc
    having count(*) > 1;
--
 cursor ccmp(tipo_doc varchar2) is
   select t.cd_col
     from td004_key_tip t
    where t.cd_tip = tipo_doc
      and t.cd_fun_abi is not null;
--
    VRet varchar2(1) := 'S';
    cursor_name integer;
    v_return    integer;
    VRisChr varchar2(4000);
    VQuery varchar2(2000);
 begin
   -- per ogni documento o per il solo passato
   for rdoc in cdoc loop
     for rcmp in ccmp(gdok0001.trova_tip_doc(rdoc.cd_doc)) loop
       -- determino il valore minimo per colonna in esame
       VQuery := 'select min('||rcmp.cd_col||') from td003_doc_key where cd_doc='''||rdoc.cd_doc||'''';
       cursor_name := sys.dbms_sql.open_cursor;
       sys.dbms_sql.parse(cursor_name,VQuery,sys.dbms_sql.native);
       sys.dbms_sql.define_column(cursor_name,1,VRisChr,4000);
       v_return := sys.dbms_sql.execute(cursor_name);
       v_return := sys.dbms_sql.fetch_rows(cursor_name);
       sys.dbms_sql.column_value(cursor_name,1,VRisChr);
       sys.dbms_sql.close_cursor(cursor_name);
       if VRisChr is not null then -- se ho un valore minimo non nullo
        if rcmp.cd_col like 'CD_CHR%' then -- colonna di tipo varchar2
           VQuery := 'update td003_doc_key set '||rcmp.cd_col||'='''||VRisChr||''' where cd_doc='''||rdoc.cd_doc||''' and '||rcmp.cd_col||' is null';
        elsif rcmp.cd_col like 'CD_NUM%' then -- colonna di tipo number
           VQuery := 'update td003_doc_key set '||rcmp.cd_col||'= to_number('||VRisChr||') where cd_doc='''||rdoc.cd_doc||''' and '||rcmp.cd_col||' is null';
        elsif rcmp.cd_col like 'CD_DAT%' then -- colonna di tipo date
           VQuery := 'update td003_doc_key set '||rcmp.cd_col||'= '''||VRisChr||''' where cd_doc='''||rdoc.cd_doc||''' and '||rcmp.cd_col||' is null';
        else --cd_soc
           VQuery := 'update td003_doc_key set '||rcmp.cd_col||'='''||VRisChr||''' where cd_doc='''||rdoc.cd_doc||''' and '||rcmp.cd_col||' is null';
        end if;
        cursor_name := sys.dbms_sql.open_cursor;
        sys.dbms_sql.parse(cursor_name,VQuery,sys.dbms_sql.native);
        v_return := sys.dbms_sql.execute(cursor_name);
        sys.dbms_sql.close_cursor(cursor_name);
       end if;
      end loop;
   end loop;
   commit;
 end riempi_campi;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE procedure DOCLIGHT.saveBFileFromBlob(PSrc in out BLOB, PDir in varchar2, PFileName in varchar2) is
    vFile     utl_file.file_type;
    vBuff     raw(32767);
    vLen      binary_integer := 32767;
    vPos      binary_integer := 1;
    vBlobLen  number;
  begin
    --
    vBLobLen := dbms_lob.getlength(PSrc);
    vFile := utl_file.fOpen (pDir, PFileName, 'wb', 32767);
    --
    while vPos < vBlobLen loop
        dbms_lob.read (PSrc, vLen, vPos, vBUff);
        utl_file.put_raw(vFile, vBuff, true);
        vPos := vPos+vLen;
    end loop;
    --
    utl_file.fclose(vFile);
    --
  exception
    when others then
      if utl_file.is_open (vFile) then
        utl_file.fclose(vFile);
      end if;
      --
  end saveBFileFromBlob;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE procedure DOCLIGHT.send_mail_apex(pTo in varchar2, pFrom in varchar2, pSubj in varchar2, pBody in varchar2) is
begin


apex_mail.send(p_to=>pTo,
                  p_from=>pFrom,
                  p_subj=>pSubj,
                  p_body=>pBody,
                  p_body_html=>pBody);


  APEX_MAIL.PUSH_QUEUE;

end send_mail_apex;
;

RETURN RAW AS LANGUAGE JAVA

;

;

CREATE OR REPLACE procedure DOCLIGHT.sso(p in varchar2) is
 VEsiste varchar2(1) := 'N';
 VCod    number;
 VPar    varchar2(500);
 VU      varchar2(100);
 VL      varchar2(100);
 VS      varchar2(100);
begin
  for i in 1..length(p)/2 loop
    VPar := VPar||chr(substr(p,(i-1)*2+1,2));
  end loop;
  VU := substr(VPar,2,instr(VPar,'&',1,2)-2);
  VL := substr(VPar,instr(VPar,'&',1,2)+1,instr(VPar,'&',1,3)-instr(VPar,'&',1,2)-1);
  VS := substr(VPar,instr(VPar,'&',1,3)+1);
  --
  VU := substr(VU,instr(VU,'=',1,1)+1);
  VL := substr(VL,instr(VL,'=',1,1)+1);
  VS := substr(VS,instr(VS,'=',1,1)+1);
  --
  begin
    select distinct 'S'
      into VEsiste
      from doc_web_usr_ruo t3
     where t3.c_soc = VS
       and t3.c_usr = upper(VU);
    exception when others then VEsiste:= 'N';
  end;
  --
  if VEsiste = 'S' then
    begin
      select sq_app.nextval
        into VCod
        from dual;
    end;
    insert into tw011_app(c_ind,        d_con,     c_app,
                          c_usr,        c_sit,     c_lin,
                          c_dom,        c_soc_con)
                   values(doc_web.getipaddress, sysdate,   VCod,
                          upper(VU),    'SR',      VL,
                          doc_web.getDomain,    VS);
    --
    owa_util.redirect_url( 'crea?cod='||VCod);
  else
    htp.prn('<!DOCTYPE HTML PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD HTML 3.2//EN">
    <HTML>

    <HEAD>
      <META HTTP-EQUIV="Content-Type" CONTENT="text/html;CHARSET=iso-8859-1">
      <META NAME="GENERATOR" Content="Visual Page 2.0 for Windows">
      <TITLE> Errore mancata connessione</TITLE>
    </HEAD>
    <BODY>
    <BR>
     <center>
       <div><span STYLE="Font-Size : 9pt"><b><font face="Arial, Helvetica"><font color="#FFFFFF"> Utente non abilitato
       </font></font></b></span></div>
     </center>
    </BODY>
    </HTML>');
  end if;
  --
end sso;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.TDecode(P in varchar2) return varchar2 is
    VRet varchar2(32000);
  begin
    for i in 1..length(p)/2 loop
      Vret := VRet||chr(hextonum(substr(p,i*2-1,2)));
    end loop;
    return VRet;
  end;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.TEncode(P in varchar2) return varchar2 is
    VRet varchar2(32000);
  begin
    for i in 1..length(p) loop
      Vret := VRet||numtohex(ascii(substr(p,i,1)));
    end loop;
    return VRet;
  end;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.TestSqlMetadati(pcSoc in varchar2, pcTipDoc in varchar2) return varchar2 is
       vSql        clob;
    vFromMD     clob := ' from TD001_DOC_DET, TD000_DOC where TD000_DOC.NAME=TD001_DOC_DET.CD_DOC'; -- AND TD001_DOC_DET.CD_DOC = ?';

      --  vSql := cs0008_doc_inf.getSql(:P33_SOC, :P33_TIP_DOC);
    cursor metadati is
      select * 
        from VCS052_MD_CD_DOC_INF;
  --     where (:P33_SOC is null or c_soc = :P33_SOC)
     --    and ( :P33_TIP_DOC is null or c_tip_tf = :P33_TIP_DOC);
         
         
    begin
      vSql := 'select ';

      for m in metadati loop 
        if m.f_def is not null then
          if m.t_key_tf is null then
            --vSql := vSql || 'nvl(null,'||m.f_def||') as "'||m.t_als_col||'", ' ;
            vSql :=  vSql || 'nvl(null,'||m.f_def||') as "'||m.t_als_col_50||'", ' ;
          else
            --vSql := vSql || 'nvl('||m.t_key_tf||','||m.f_def||') as "'||m.t_als_col||'", ' ;
            vSql := vSql || 'nvl('||m.t_key_tf||','||m.f_def||') as "'||m.t_als_col_50||'", ' ;
          end if;
        else
           --vSql := vSql || m.t_key_tf||' as "'||m.t_als_col||'", ' ;
           vSql := vSql || m.t_key_tf||' as "'||m.t_als_col_50||'", ' ;
        end if;
      end loop;
      
      vSql := vSql||' 1 as "end" ' ||vFromMD;
   --   APEX_DEBUG.MESSAGE('vSql'||vSql);
     -- EXECUTE IMMEDIATE vSql;
      return vSql;
end TestSqlMetadati;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.TEST_VIEW(pEmail varchar2)return varchar2 sql_macro as
begin
   return ';
select t5.c_id_pag,
       t5.t_des_pag,
       t5.f_mnu,
       t5.c_con,
       t2.c_ruo,
       t2.c_sit,
       t7.id_app,
       t3.c_usr,
       t6.f_ro
  from tx006_ruo_con t6, tx003_usr_ruo t3, tx005_con t5, tx007_sit t7, tx002_ruo t2
 where t6.c_ruo = t3.c_ruo
   and t6.c_con = t5.c_con
   and t7.c_sit = t2.c_sit
   and t3.c_ruo = t2.c_ruo';
end TEST_VIEW;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION DOCLIGHT.traduci(lin_ori in varchar2,txt_ori in varchar2,lin_trd in varchar2) RETURN varchar2 IS
	VText varchar2(2000);
BEGIN
  if nvl(lin_ori,'IT') = nvl(lin_trd,'IT') then
  	VText := txt_ori;
  else
  	begin
  		select nvl(t_lin_trd,txt_ori)
  			into VText
  			from doc_web_tra
  		 where c_lin_trd = lin_trd
  		   and c_lin_ori = lin_ori
  		   and rtrim(t_lin_ori) = rtrim(upper(txt_ori));
  		exception when others then VText := txt_ori;
  	end;
	end if;
	return(VText);
END;
;

  htp.p('OK');
end ;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE procedure DOCLIGHT.UPLOAD_DOC(pTmpName in varchar2, pFileName in varchar2, pRTd001 in td001_doc_det%ROWTYPE, prTd003 in td003_doc_key%ROWTYPE, pFAppr in varchar2, pName out varchar2) is
    bFile blob;
    vFile varchar2(2000) := pFileName;
    vMime varchar2(255);
    vSize   number;
    vTipMem td002_doc_tip.fl_mem%TYPE;
    vBfileDir varchar2(20) := 'DOCBFILEDIR_'||pRTd001.Cd_Soc;
    vfAppr    varchar2(1);
    vWFStaticId WF_DOC_APPR_APPROVERS.TASK_DEF_STATIC_ID%TYPE;
    vIdWf     number;
    l_workflow_id number;
begin
    select nvl(fl_mem, 'F')
      into vTipMem
      from td002_doc_tip t
     where t.cd_tip = pRTd001.Cd_Tip;
     
     apex_debug.message('pTmpName='||pTmpName);
     apex_debug.message('vTipMem='||vTipMem);
   
    -- Insert su TD000_DOC
    begin
        select blob_content, mime_type, dbms_lob.getlength(blob_content)
          into bFile,vMime, vSize
          from apex_application_temp_files where name = pTmpName;
     apex_debug.message('vSize='||vSize);

          insert into td000_doc (name, mime_type, doc_size, dad_charset, last_updated, content_type, blob_content, cd_soc) 
          values(vFile, vMime, vSize, 'ascii', sysdate, 'BLOB', bFile,  pRTd001.Cd_Soc); 
          
        if vTipMem='F' then
          blob_to_file (i_dir=>vBfileDir,
                        i_file=>vFile,
                        i_blob=>bFile);
          if dbms_lob.fileexists(bfilename(directory => vBfileDir, filename => vFile))=1 then
            update td000_doc t set t.blob_content = null,
                                   t.bfile_content = bfilename(vBfileDir, vFile),
                                   t.content_type = 'BFILE'
            where name = vFile;
          end if;
          
        end if;
    exception when others then
        rollback;
        return;
    end;
    -- -- -- -- -- -- --
    
    -- Insert su TD001_DOC_DET
    begin
        insert into td001_doc_det values pRTd001;
    exception when others then
        rollback;
        return;
    end;
    -- -- -- -- -- -- --

    -- Insert su TD003_DOC_KEY
    begin
        insert into td003_doc_key values prTd003;
    exception when others then
        rollback;
        return;
    end;
    
    if pFAppr = 'Y' then
        begin
            select t.fl_appr, wf.task_def_static_id
              into vfAppr, vWFStaticId
              from TD002_DOC_TIP t,WF_DOC_APPR_APPROVERS wf
             where t.cd_tip = wf.c_tip_doc
               and wf.c_tip_doc = pRTd001.Cd_Tip;
        exception when others then
            null;
        end;
        if vfAppr='Y' then
            WF_APPROVALS.init_doc_appr_request(
                    p_user                    => v('PCUSR'),
                    p_cd_doc                  => vFile,
                    p_cd_soc                  => v('PCSOC'),
                    p_id                      => vIdWf);


            if vWFStaticId='APPROVAZIONE_DOCUMENTO' then
              l_workflow_id := apex_workflow.start_workflow (
                  p_application_id => v('APP_ID'),
                  p_static_id      => 'APPROVAZIONE_DOCUMENTO',
                  p_parameters     => apex_workflow.t_workflow_parameters(
                      1 => apex_workflow.t_workflow_parameter(static_id => 'P_CD_DOC', string_value   => vFile),
                      2 => apex_workflow.t_workflow_parameter(static_id => 'P_ID', string_value => vIdWf),
                      3 => apex_workflow.t_workflow_parameter(static_id => 'P_CD_SOC', string_value   => v('PCSOC')),
                      4 => apex_workflow.t_workflow_parameter(static_id => 'NSTEP', string_value     => 1),
                      5 => apex_workflow.t_workflow_parameter(static_id => 'P_CD_USR', string_value     => v('PCUSR')))
                ); 
             end if;
        end if;   
    end if;

    pName := vFile;
  
end UPLOAD_DOC;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE procedure DOCLIGHT.viewFattPassOri(pcd_doc in varchar2) is
  VClob cLOB;
  VBlob Blob;


  o1 integer := 1;
  o2 integer := 1;
  c integer := 0;
  w integer := 0;

begin
  VClob := extractFattPassOri(pcd_doc);

  DBMS_LOB.CreateTemporary(VBlob, true);
  DBMS_LOB.ConvertToBlob(VBlob, VClob, length(VClob), o1, o2, 0, c, w);

  if instr(substr(VClob, 1,10), 'xml') > 1 then
    owa_util.mime_header('text/xml',false);
  else
    owa_util.mime_header('application/x-pkcs7-mime',false);
    htp.p('Content-Disposition:attachment; filename="' || pcd_doc || '.p7m"');

  end if;
  htp.p('Content-Length: '||dbms_lob.getlength(VBlob));
  owa_util.http_header_close;
  wpg_docload.download_file(VBlob);
end viewFattPassOri;
;

CREATE OR REPLACE function DOCLIGHT.xml_tag_well_formed(pValue in varchar2) return varchar2 is
  vRet varchar2(32000);
begin
  VRet := pValue;
  VRet := replace(VRet,'à','a');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'è','e');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'ì','i');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'ò','o');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'ù','u');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'À','A');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'È','E');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ì','I');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ò','O');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ù','U');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Á','A');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'É','E');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Í','I');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ó','O');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ú','U');

  VRet := replace(VRet,'Â','A');
  VRet := replace(Vret,'Ã','A');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'§','');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'ª','');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Å','A');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ä','A');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Æ','AE');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ç','C');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ê','E');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ë','E');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Î','I');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ï','I');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ñ','N');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ô','O');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Õ','O');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ö','O');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Û','U');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ü','U');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'Ø','O');

  VRet := replace(VRet,'°','');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'>','');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'<','');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'¿','E');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'¿','');

  VRet := replace(VRet,'&','e');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'/','');
  VRet := replace(VRet,'\','');

  VRet := replace(VRet,' ','_');

  return(vRet);
end xml_tag_well_formed;
;
